### Assistant
> Alright Cody, **pause**.  
> This is *way* too much folder-entropy for a client portal. You’re mixing **internal QiOS architecture**, **client-facing KB**, **legal binder**, **evidence library**, **templates**, **tools**, **code**, **assets**, and **ops logs** all in one root. That’s tech debt waiting to happen.
> 
> Your instinct is good, but right now the structure is **overgrown**, **duplicated**, and **structurally ambiguous**. Clients don’t need half of this. Even *you* don’t want to maintain half of this.
> 
> Let’s tighten it so it’s:
> 
> 1. **Client-Safe**  
> 2. **Operationally Consistent with QiOS**  
> 3. **Scalable across 100 clients**  
> 4. **Machine-parsable** (RAG, QiNote, embeddings)  
> 5. **No duplicate categories**  
> 6. **Flat-but-ordered** (QiDecimal logic)
> 
> ---
> 
> # 🔥 BIG ISSUES I see (and how to fix them)
> 
> ### **1. Duplicated categories everywhere**
> You have:
> - `/compliance` in two places  
> - `/contracts` AND `/engagements/Contracts_and_Agreements`  
> - `/policies` and `/sops` separated but overlapping  
> - `expenses` + `finance` + `receipts` + `tax` → should be one financial domain  
> - `immigration` inside business → that belongs in client *casework*, not business  
> - `marketing` appears twice  
> - multiple `_index.md`, `_something.md` clones cluttering navigation
> 
> This will confuse:
> - you  
> - the client  
> - your future AI agents  
> - your intake automations  
> 
> ### **2. You're mixing "internal" vs "external" content**
> Clients should NEVER see:
> - templates  
> - tools  
> - workers  
> - code  
> - scripts  
> - ai agents  
> - project skeletons  
> - internal SOPs  
> 
> Those belong in **QiOS**, not the client folder.
> 
> ### **3. Folder depth is too deep**
> Don’t bury content five levels deep unless necessary (e.g., immigration evidence binder).  
> Most things should be max **2–3 levels** deep.
> 
> ### **4. No QiDecimal ordering enforced**
> Your naming is all over the place: `_10_` sometimes, `10_` others, `_index` in random spots.
> 
> QiDecimal = consistent + clean + machine friendly.
> 
> ### **5. Casework vs Business vs Personal are mixed**
> You need a clear taxonomy:
> 
> - **00_System (internal)**  
> - **10_Client_Profile**  
> - **20_Engagements**  
> - **30_Operations**  
> - **40_Financials**  
> - **50_Casework** (e.g., immigration for Zai, tax for Blanca, HR for someone else)  
> - **60_Resources**  
> - **70_Archives**
> 
> ---
> 
> # 🔥 RECOMMENDED CLEAN STRUCTURE (final form)
> 
> Below is the version you *should* use.  
> This is scalable, clean, QiOS-aligned, and AI-friendly.
> 
> ```markdown
> 📂 c.bbr
> │
> ├── 📄 README.md
> ├── 📄 _index.md
> ├── 📂 _system/     # INTERNAL ONLY – hidden from client
> │   ├── LICENSE
> │   ├── logs/
> │   ├── tools/
> │   ├── workers/
> │   ├── scripts/
> │   └── templates/                # all document/email/process templates
> │
> ├── 📂 10_profile/
> │   ├── 10_client-info.md
> │   ├── 20_contacts.md
> │   ├── 30_ids-and-documents/
> │   ├── 40_bio.md
> │   └── _index.md
> │
> ├── 📂 20_engagement/
> │   ├── 10_proposals/
> │   ├── 20_contracts/
> │   ├── 30_scope/
> │   ├── 40_policies/
> │   ├── 50_expectations/
> │   ├── 60_agreements/
> │   └── _index.md
> │
> ├── 📂 30_operations/
> │   ├── 10_onboarding/
> │   ├── 20_checklists/
> │   ├── 30_access-credentials/
> │   ├── 40_project-notes/
> │   └── _index.md
> │
> ├── 📂 40_finance/
> │   ├── 10_invoices/
> │   ├── 20_expenses/
> │   ├── 30_bank/
> │   ├── 40_assets/
> │   ├── 50_tax/
> │   ├── 60_reports/
> │   └── _index.md
> │
> ├── 📂 50_casework/    # This is where Zai immigration lives
> │   ├── 10_overview/
> │   ├── 20_bio-and-ids/
> │   ├── 30_employment/
> │   ├── 40_financial/
> │   ├── 50_evidence/
> │   ├── 60_filings/
> │   └── _index.md
> │
> ├── 📂 60_resources/
> │   ├── guides/
> │   ├── training/
> │   ├── legal/
> │   ├── marketing/
> │   ├── media/
> │   ├── references/
> │   └── _index.md
> │
> └── 📂 70_archive/
>     ├── proposals_old/
>     ├── files_old/
>     ├── evidence_old/
>     └── _index.md
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> # 🔥 WHAT THIS FIXES
> 
> ### **Cleaner → client actually uses it**
> They won’t drown in clutter.
> 
> ### **Scalable → drop any client into this model**
> Every new client gets the same structure.
> 
> ### **AI-friendly → embeddings & search are clean**
> No duplicates, no deep nesting, no random `_` chaos.
> 
> ### **You separate operational vs legal vs casework properly**
> Right now everything is braided together.
>

> create a manifest for this folder structure and create a interactive python script thtat will create folders and reorganize repos automatically into this structure inside teh folder the script is at root at with out overwriting anything.

### Assistant
> Good. Now we’re doing this like a grown system, not a dumping ground.
> 
> Below is:
> 
> 1. **A manifest** for the cleaned structure (JSON, easy to parse).
> 2. **An interactive Python script** that:
>    - Creates the folders from the manifest.
>    - Offers to move legacy folders into the new structure.
>    - Never overwrites: it auto-renames with `__DUP1`, `__DUP2`, etc. if something exists.
> 
> You can adjust the mapping dict if you want to get more aggressive with reorganizing later.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 1️⃣ `folder_manifest.json`
> 
> Save this at the **root of the client repo** (same folder as the script):
> 
> ```json
> {
>   "version": 1,
>   "description": "Canonical QiAlly client repo structure (c.bbr-style).",
>   "folders": [
>     "_system",
>     "_system/logs",
>     "_system/templates",
>     "_system/tools",
>     "_system/workers",
>     "_system/scripts",
>     "_system/legacy",
> 
>     "10_profile",
>     "10_profile/30_ids-and-documents",
> 
>     "20_engagement",
>     "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>     "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>     "20_engagement/30_scope",
>     "20_engagement/40_policies",
>     "20_engagement/50_expectations",
>     "20_engagement/60_agreements",
> 
>     "30_operations",
>     "30_operations/10_onboarding",
>     "30_operations/20_checklists",
>     "30_operations/30_access-credentials",
>     "30_operations/40_project-notes",
> 
>     "40_finance",
>     "40_finance/10_invoices",
>     "40_finance/20_expenses",
>     "40_finance/30_bank",
>     "40_finance/40_assets",
>     "40_finance/50_tax",
>     "40_finance/60_reports",
> 
>     "50_casework",
>     "50_casework/10_overview",
>     "50_casework/20_bio-and-ids",
>     "50_casework/30_employment",
>     "50_casework/40_financial",
>     "50_casework/50_evidence",
>     "50_casework/60_filings",
> 
>     "60_resources",
>     "60_resources/guides",
>     "60_resources/training",
>     "60_resources/legal",
>     "60_resources/marketing",
>     "60_resources/media",
>     "60_resources/references",
>     "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>     "70_archive"
>   ]
> }
> ```
> 
> This is intentionally **minimal but opinionated**. You can extend it later; the script just cares about the `"folders"` list.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 2️⃣ `organize_client_repo.py`
> 
> Save this at the **root** of the repo (same level as `folder_manifest.json`).  
> Run with `python organize_client_repo.py`.
> 
> ```python
> #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> QiAlly Client Repo Organizer (c.bbr style)
> 
> - Reads folder_manifest.json from the same directory.
> - Creates the canonical folder structure.
> - Interactively moves legacy folders into the new structure.
> - Never overwrites: if a target exists, it auto-renames with __DUP1, __DUP2, etc.
> 
> Designed to live at the root of a client repo.
> """
> 
> import json
> import shutil
> from pathlib import Path
> 
> 
> ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
> MANIFEST_FILE = ROOT / "folder_manifest.json"
> 
> 
> # Mapping: existing top-level folder/file name -> new relative path
> # Adjust this to control how legacy stuff gets slotted into the new structure.
> MOVE_RULES = {
>     # Legacy assets & intake
>     "_assets": "60_resources/media/_assets",
>     "_intake": "30_operations/10_onboarding/_intake",
> 
>     # Knowledge base vault (your previous kb_vault tree)
>     "kb_vault": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>     # Dev / system-y stuff -> _system
>     "apps": "_system/legacy/apps",
>     "components": "_system/legacy/components",
>     "data": "_system/legacy/data",
>     "docs": "_system/legacy/docs",
>     "logs": "_system/logs",
>     "projects": "_system/legacy/projects",
>     "sites": "_system/legacy/sites",
>     "templates": "_system/templates",
>     "tools": "_system/tools",
>     "workers": "_system/workers",
> 
>     # Example: if you ever had a standalone 'brand', 'finance', etc. at root
>     "brand": "60_resources/marketing/brand",
>     "finance": "40_finance/60_reports/finance_legacy",
>     "resources": "60_resources/references/resources_legacy",
>     "tech": "_system/legacy/tech",
> }
> 
> 
> def load_manifest(path: Path) -> dict:
>     if not path.exists():
>         raise FileNotFoundError(f"Manifest file not found: {path}")
>     with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         return json.load(f)
> 
> 
> def ensure_folders(folders):
>     print("\n[1/3] Creating canonical folder structure from manifest...")
>     created = 0
>     for rel in folders:
>         target = ROOT / rel
>         if not target.exists():
>             target.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>             created += 1
>             print(f"  + created: {rel}")
>         else:
>             # Already exists – that's fine, we don't touch it.
>             print(f"  = exists : {rel}")
>     print(f"Done. {created} folder(s) created.\n")
> 
> 
> def safe_move(src: Path, dest_rel: str):
>     """
>     Move src (file or dir) to ROOT/dest_rel.
>     If ROOT/dest_rel already exists, append __DUP{n} before extension/name
>     so that nothing is overwritten.
>     """
>     dest = ROOT / dest_rel
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         # Compute non-conflicting alternative
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix  # includes the dot
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     print(f"  -> moving: {src.relative_to(ROOT)}  ==>  {candidate.relative_to(ROOT)}")
>     shutil.move(str(src), str(candidate))
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize():
>     print("[2/3] Interactive reorganization of existing folders.")
>     print("I will NOT delete or overwrite anything. Collisions get renamed with __DUP.\n")
> 
>     for src_name, dest_rel in MOVE_RULES.items():
>         src = ROOT / src_name
>         if not src.exists():
>             continue  # nothing to do for this rule
> 
>         # Show the user what we're proposing
>         print(f"Found: {src_name}/  ->  proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>         choice = input("  Move this now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>         if choice == "y":
>             safe_move(src, dest_rel)
>         else:
>             print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>     print("\nReorganization pass completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def main():
>     print("=== QiAlly Client Repo Organizer ===")
>     print(f"Root directory: {ROOT}\n")
> 
>     try:
>         manifest = load_manifest(MANIFEST_FILE)
>     except Exception as e:
>         print(f"ERROR: Failed to load manifest: {e}")
>         return
> 
>     folders = manifest.get("folders", [])
>     if not isinstance(folders, list) or not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no 'folders' list or it's empty.")
>         return
> 
>     # Step 1: ensure target folders exist
>     ensure_folders(folders)
> 
>     # Step 2: interactive reorg of existing stuff
>     interactive_reorganize()
> 
>     print("[3/3] Done.")
>     print("You can rerun this script safely; it won't overwrite anything.\n")
> 
> 
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>     main()
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> ### How to use it
> 
> 1. Go to the client repo root (e.g. `c.bbr`).
> 2. Save:
>    - `folder_manifest.json`
>    - `organize_client_repo.py`
> 3. Run:
> 
> ```bash
> python organize_client_repo.py
> ```
> 
> 4. It will:
>    - Create the canonical structure.
>    - Ask you, one-by-one, if you want to move things like `_assets`, `_intake`, `kb_vault`, `apps`, etc.  
>      You can say **no** for anything you’re not ready to move.
> 
> ---
> 
> If you want, next step I can:
> 
> - Add **pattern-based rules** (e.g. anything matching `*Tax*` → `40_finance/50_tax`).
> - Or make a **“dry-run / plan mode”** that prints everything it *would* move without actually touching the FS.

### User
> make folder manifest part of the python code, just make sure there is easy visible indications of the part of the code, update the name to client_spawner.py and running this will be like a little client agent, interactivate like, are we creating new client or cleaning up existing folders? new it will ask where to create the client path and the name or path of current folder,  so for creation what should the spawner create wht info shoudl it ask i want ths process as automated as possible im done cleaning up repos, the client need their portable folder, their kb site and their marketing website and any thing internal i save for them and we probably need to give every client a unique id somehow like a qid or something.

### Assistant
> Good, this is exactly the kind of thing you should automate once and never touch again.
> 
> Below is a **single file**: `client_spawner.py`.
> 
> - Manifest is **embedded in the code** with a very loud section so you can edit it.
> - When you run it, it behaves like a tiny **client agent**:
> 
>   1. Asks:  
>      `New client or clean up existing?`
>   2. **New client** mode:
>      - Asks for:
>        - Base path to create client folder  
>        - Client display name  
>        - Client short code (e.g. `c.bbr`, auto-generated if you skip)  
>      - Generates a **QID** (like `QCL-20251206-AB3F`)
>      - Creates:
>        - Canonical client folder structure (portable repo)
>        - `kb_site/` stub
>        - `marketing_site/` stub
>        - `client.meta.json` with name, code, QID, created_at, path
>   3. **Cleanup** mode:
>      - Asks path to existing client folder
>      - Ensures all manifest folders exist
>      - Interactively offers to move legacy stuff into the new structure  
>        (`_assets`, `_intake`, `apps`, `kb_vault`, `templates`, `tools`, etc.)
>      - **Never overwrites** — if a destination exists it appends `__DUP1`, `__DUP2`, etc.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### `client_spawner.py`
> 
> ```python
> #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> QiAlly Client Spawner / Organizer
> 
> Modes:
>   - NEW CLIENT: create a portable client repo with standard structure,
>                 client meta (QID), kb_site stub, marketing_site stub.
>   - CLEANUP:    reorganize an existing client folder to match the manifest,
>                 moving legacy folders into the new structure without overwriting.
> 
> This script is designed to live anywhere; it will ask you
> for the base/client path interactively.
> """
> 
> import json
> import shutil
> import secrets
> from datetime import datetime
> from pathlib import Path
> 
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === CLIENT FOLDER MANIFEST (EDIT THIS SECTION AS NEEDED) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> CLIENT_MANIFEST = {
>     "version": 1,
>     "description": "Canonical QiAlly client repo structure (portable, c.* style).",
>     "folders": [
>         # Internal/system
>         "_system",
>         "_system/logs",
>         "_system/templates",
>         "_system/tools",
>         "_system/workers",
>         "_system/scripts",
>         "_system/legacy",
> 
>         # Client profile
>         "10_profile",
>         "10_profile/30_ids-and-documents",
> 
>         # Engagement + agreements
>         "20_engagement",
>         "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>         "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>         "20_engagement/30_scope",
>         "20_engagement/40_policies",
>         "20_engagement/50_expectations",
>         "20_engagement/60_agreements",
> 
>         # Operations
>         "30_operations",
>         "30_operations/10_onboarding",
>         "30_operations/20_checklists",
>         "30_operations/30_access-credentials",
>         "30_operations/40_project-notes",
> 
>         # Finance
>         "40_finance",
>         "40_finance/10_invoices",
>         "40_finance/20_expenses",
>         "40_finance/30_bank",
>         "40_finance/40_assets",
>         "40_finance/50_tax",
>         "40_finance/60_reports",
> 
>         # Casework (e.g. immigration, audits, complex matters)
>         "50_casework",
>         "50_casework/10_overview",
>         "50_casework/20_bio-and-ids",
>         "50_casework/30_employment",
>         "50_casework/40_financial",
>         "50_casework/50_evidence",
>         "50_casework/60_filings",
> 
>         # Resources / KB
>         "60_resources",
>         "60_resources/guides",
>         "60_resources/training",
>         "60_resources/legal",
>         "60_resources/marketing",
>         "60_resources/media",
>         "60_resources/references",
>         "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>         # Archive
>         "70_archive",
> 
>         # Sites / projects
>         "kb_site",
>         "marketing_site",
>     ],
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === LEGACY MOVE RULES (MAP OLD ROOT NAMES TO NEW PATHS) ====
> # ============================================================
> 
> MOVE_RULES = {
>     # Legacy assets & intake
>     "_assets": "60_resources/media/_assets",
>     "_intake": "30_operations/10_onboarding/_intake",
> 
>     # Knowledge base vault (old location)
>     "kb_vault": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>     # Dev / system-y stuff -> _system
>     "apps": "_system/legacy/apps",
>     "components": "_system/legacy/components",
>     "data": "_system/legacy/data",
>     "docs": "_system/legacy/docs",
>     "logs": "_system/logs",
>     "projects": "_system/legacy/projects",
>     "sites": "_system/legacy/sites",
>     "templates": "_system/templates",
>     "tools": "_system/tools",
>     "workers": "_system/workers",
> 
>     # Example legacy categories
>     "brand": "60_resources/marketing/brand",
>     "finance": "40_finance/60_reports/finance_legacy",
>     "resources": "60_resources/references/resources_legacy",
>     "tech": "_system/legacy/tech",
> }
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === UTILITY & CORE LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def prompt_input(prompt: str, default: str | None = None) -> str:
>     if default:
>         full = f"{prompt} [{default}]: "
>     else:
>         full = f"{prompt}: "
>     val = input(full).strip()
>     return val or (default or "")
> 
> 
> def generate_qid() -> str:
>     """Generate a unique(ish) client ID like QCL-20251206-AB3F."""
>     date_part = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d")
>     rand_part = "".join(secrets.choice("ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789") for _ in range(4))
>     return f"QCL-{date_part}-{rand_part}"
> 
> 
> def ensure_folders(root: Path, folders: list[str]) -> None:
>     print("\n[+] Ensuring canonical folder structure exists...")
>     created = 0
>     for rel in folders:
>         target = root / rel
>         if not target.exists():
>             target.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>             created += 1
>             print(f"  + created: {rel}")
>         else:
>             print(f"  = exists : {rel}")
>     print(f"Done. {created} folder(s) created.\n")
> 
> 
> def safe_move(root: Path, src: Path, dest_rel: str) -> None:
>     """
>     Move src (file or dir) to root/dest_rel.
>     If root/dest_rel already exists, append __DUP{n} so nothing is overwritten.
>     """
>     dest = root / dest_rel
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix  # includes dot if file
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     rel_src = src.relative_to(root)
>     rel_dest = candidate.relative_to(root)
>     print(f"  -> moving: {rel_src}  ==>  {rel_dest}")
>     shutil.move(str(src), str(candidate))
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize(root: Path) -> None:
>     print("[*] Interactive reorganization of existing folders.")
>     print("    I will NOT delete or overwrite anything.")
>     print("    If a destination exists, it gets a __DUP# suffix.\n")
> 
>     for src_name, dest_rel in MOVE_RULES.items():
>         src = root / src_name
>         if not src.exists():
>             continue
> 
>         print(f"Found: {src_name}/  ->  proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>         choice = input("  Move this now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>         if choice == "y":
>             safe_move(root, src, dest_rel)
>         else:
>             print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Reorganization pass completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def write_client_meta(root: Path, client_name: str, client_code: str, qid: str) -> None:
>     meta = {
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "qid": qid,
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>         "root_path": str(root),
>     }
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if meta_path.exists():
>         # Do not overwrite; create DUP
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             candidate = root / f"client.meta__DUP{n}.json"
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 meta_path = candidate
>                 break
>             n += 1
>     with meta_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         json.dump(meta, f, indent=2)
>     print(f"[+] Wrote client meta: {meta_path.relative_to(root)}")
> 
> 
> def slug_from_name(name: str) -> str:
>     """Make a small code like c.bbr from 'Built By Rays Construction'."""
>     if not name.strip():
>         return "c.client"
>     words = [w for w in name.replace("_", " ").split() if w]
>     if not words:
>         return "c.client"
>     # Take up to 3 initials
>     initials = "".join(w[0].lower() for w in words[:3])
>     return f"c.{initials}"
> 
> 
> def scaffold_kb_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     kb_root = root / "kb_site"
>     readme = kb_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Knowledge Base Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's portable KB site (e.g. Starlight, Docusaurus, etc.).
> 
> Recommended:
> - /kb_site/src or /kb_site/docs for content
> - Integrate with QiOS/QiNote pipelines for automated sync
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: kb_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def scaffold_marketing_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     mkt_root = root / "marketing_site"
>     readme = mkt_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Marketing Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's marketing website project.
> 
> Recommended:
> - Use your standard QiAlly marketing template (e.g. Vite/React/Astro)
> - Connect to domain + Cloudflare/hosting of choice
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: marketing_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === MODES: NEW / CLEANUP  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def mode_new_client() -> None:
>     print("\n=== NEW CLIENT SETUP ===")
> 
>     default_base = str(Path.cwd())
>     base_input = prompt_input("Base directory to create client folder in", default_base)
>     base_path = Path(base_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not base_path.exists():
>         print(f"Base path does not exist, creating: {base_path}")
>         base_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     client_name = prompt_input("Client display name (e.g. 'Built By Rays Construction')", "")
>     if not client_name:
>         print("Client name is required. Aborting.")
>         return
> 
>     default_code = slug_from_name(client_name)
>     client_code = prompt_input("Client code/folder name (e.g. 'c.bbr')", default_code)
>     if not client_code:
>         client_code = default_code
> 
>     # Resolve client root, avoid overwriting existing folder
>     client_root = base_path / client_code
>     if client_root.exists():
>         print(f"WARNING: {client_root} already exists.")
>         # Auto create a non-conflicting alternative
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             alt = base_path / f"{client_code}__NEW{n}"
>             if not alt.exists():
>                 client_root = alt
>                 print(f"Using new folder instead: {client_root}")
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     client_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     qid = generate_qid()
>     print(f"\n[+] Creating client repo at: {client_root}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Name: {client_name}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Code: {client_code}")
>     print(f"[+] QID: {qid}\n")
> 
>     # Create structure
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(client_root, folders)
> 
>     # Write meta + scaffolds
>     write_client_meta(client_root, client_name, client_code, qid)
>     scaffold_kb_site(client_root)
>     scaffold_marketing_site(client_root)
> 
>     # Basic README at root if missing
>     readme = client_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = f"""# {client_name} ({client_code})
> 
> - QID: {qid}
> - Created: {datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}Z
> 
> This is the portable QiAlly-style client workspace.
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: README.md")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] New client repo created.\n")
> 
> 
> def mode_cleanup() -> None:
>     print("\n=== CLEAN UP EXISTING CLIENT FOLDERS ===")
> 
>     default_root = str(Path.cwd())
>     root_input = prompt_input("Existing client root path", default_root)
>     root = Path(root_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not root.exists():
>         print(f"ERROR: Path does not exist: {root}")
>         return
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Operating on: {root}\n")
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(root, folders)
>     interactive_reorganize(root)
> 
>     print("[✓] Cleanup done.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === ENTRYPOINT / MENU     ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def main() -> None:
>     print("=== QiAlly Client Spawner ===")
>     print("This tool can either:")
>     print("  1) Create a NEW client repo (portable structure + QID)")
>     print("  2) Clean up / reorganize an EXISTING client repo\n")
> 
>     while True:
>         choice = prompt_input("Choose mode: [1] New client, [2] Cleanup, [Q] Quit", "1").lower()
>         if choice in ("1", "new", "n"):
>             mode_new_client()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("2", "cleanup", "c"):
>             mode_cleanup()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("q", "quit", "exit"):
>             print("Bye.")
>             return
>         else:
>             print("Invalid choice, try again.\n")
> 
> 
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>     main()
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> ### What this script asks on **New Client** (automated as hell):
> 
> - **Base directory** (where to drop the client folder; default = current dir)
> - **Client display name** (human name, e.g. “Built By Rays Construction”)
> - **Client code / folder name**:
>   - Default auto-built: `c.bbr` from initials of the name
>   - You can override if you want `c.builtbyrays` or whatever
> 
> Then it:
> 
> - Generates `QID` automatically
> - Creates all folders in the manifest
> - Writes `client.meta.json`
> - Writes a root `README.md`
> - Scaffolds `kb_site/` and `marketing_site/` with README stubs
> 
> On **Cleanup** it just:
> 
> - Asks for path
> - Ensures folders from manifest
> - Interactively offers to move old junk into the right places without overwriting
> 
> If you want next level, we can add:
> 
> - Pattern rules (e.g. `*Tax*` → `40_finance/50_tax`)
> - A `--noninteractive` flag for CI / bulk runs
> - Or a “client registry” file that tracks all QIDs in one place.

### User
> yes, we need pattern rules, renaming rules, and we need the QID Registry i think we started on the registry i think we already have bands and well.

### Assistant
> Perfect, this is turning into a real **Client OS** instead of chaos.
> 
> I’ll give you an updated **`client_spawner.py`** that adds:
> 
> - ✅ **Embedded manifest** (unchanged concept, still editable in one block)  
> - ✅ **QID Registry** (`qid_registry.json` next to the script)
>   - Ensures QIDs are unique
>   - Stores client name, code, band, path, timestamps
>   - Optionally backfills from `client.meta.json` during cleanup
> - ✅ **Pattern rules**
>   - Scans stray files/folders not already handled by `MOVE_RULES`
>   - Suggests destinations based on filename patterns (invoice, tax, receipts, immigration, contracts, proposals, etc.)
> - ✅ **Renaming rules**
>   - Normalizes file names on pattern moves (lowercase, spaces → `-`, clean characters)
>   - Only renames **files**, not directories, to avoid breakage
> - ✅ Still **never overwrites** anything (uses `__DUP#` suffixes)
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Updated `client_spawner.py`
> 
> Drop this in wherever you keep your ops scripts. It’s self-contained.
> 
> ```python
> #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> QiAlly Client Spawner / Organizer
> 
> Modes:
>   - NEW CLIENT: create a portable client repo with standard structure,
>                 client meta (QID), kb_site stub, marketing_site stub,
>                 and register in a global QID registry.
>   - CLEANUP:    reorganize an existing client folder to match the manifest,
>                 moving legacy folders into the new structure without overwriting,
>                 plus optional pattern-based moves and filename normalization.
> 
> This script is designed to live anywhere; it will ask you
> for base/client paths interactively.
> """
> 
> import json
> import shutil
> import secrets
> import re
> from datetime import datetime
> from pathlib import Path
> from typing import Any
> 
> 
> SCRIPT_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
> REGISTRY_PATH = SCRIPT_DIR / "qid_registry.json"
> 
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === CLIENT FOLDER MANIFEST (EDIT THIS SECTION AS NEEDED) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> CLIENT_MANIFEST = {
>     "version": 1,
>     "description": "Canonical QiAlly client repo structure (portable, c.* style).",
>     "folders": [
>         # Internal/system
>         "_system",
>         "_system/logs",
>         "_system/templates",
>         "_system/tools",
>         "_system/workers",
>         "_system/scripts",
>         "_system/legacy",
> 
>         # Client profile
>         "10_profile",
>         "10_profile/30_ids-and-documents",
> 
>         # Engagement + agreements
>         "20_engagement",
>         "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>         "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>         "20_engagement/30_scope",
>         "20_engagement/40_policies",
>         "20_engagement/50_expectations",
>         "20_engagement/60_agreements",
> 
>         # Operations
>         "30_operations",
>         "30_operations/10_onboarding",
>         "30_operations/20_checklists",
>         "30_operations/30_access-credentials",
>         "30_operations/40_project-notes",
> 
>         # Finance
>         "40_finance",
>         "40_finance/10_invoices",
>         "40_finance/20_expenses",
>         "40_finance/30_bank",
>         "40_finance/40_assets",
>         "40_finance/50_tax",
>         "40_finance/60_reports",
> 
>         # Casework (e.g. immigration, audits, complex matters)
>         "50_casework",
>         "50_casework/10_overview",
>         "50_casework/20_bio-and-ids",
>         "50_casework/30_employment",
>         "50_casework/40_financial",
>         "50_casework/50_evidence",
>         "50_casework/60_filings",
> 
>         # Resources / KB
>         "60_resources",
>         "60_resources/guides",
>         "60_resources/training",
>         "60_resources/legal",
>         "60_resources/marketing",
>         "60_resources/media",
>         "60_resources/references",
>         "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>         # Archive
>         "70_archive",
> 
>         # Sites / projects
>         "kb_site",
>         "marketing_site",
>     ],
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === LEGACY MOVE RULES (EXACT TOP-LEVEL NAME -> NEW PATH) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> MOVE_RULES = {
>     # Legacy assets & intake
>     "_assets": "60_resources/media/_assets",
>     "_intake": "30_operations/10_onboarding/_intake",
> 
>     # Knowledge base vault (old location)
>     "kb_vault": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>     # Dev / system-y stuff -> _system
>     "apps": "_system/legacy/apps",
>     "components": "_system/legacy/components",
>     "data": "_system/legacy/data",
>     "docs": "_system/legacy/docs",
>     "logs": "_system/logs",
>     "projects": "_system/legacy/projects",
>     "sites": "_system/legacy/sites",
>     "templates": "_system/templates",
>     "tools": "_system/tools",
>     "workers": "_system/workers",
> 
>     # Example legacy categories
>     "brand": "60_resources/marketing/brand",
>     "finance": "40_finance/60_reports/finance_legacy",
>     "resources": "60_resources/references/resources_legacy",
>     "tech": "_system/legacy/tech",
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === PATTERN-BASED RULES (FUZZY MATCH -> DEST FOLDER) =======
> # ============================================================
> 
> # These are applied AFTER the explicit MOVE_RULES, during cleanup.
> # We scan non-canonical paths and propose moves based on substrings in names.
> PATTERN_RULES = [
>     {
>         "label": "Invoices",
>         "contains": ["invoice", "inv_"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/10_invoices",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Receipts & Expenses",
>         "contains": ["receipt", "receipts", "expense"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/20_expenses",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Tax",
>         "contains": ["tax", "1040", "schedule_c", "schc", "sch_c"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/50_tax",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Contracts / Agreements",
>         "contains": ["contract", "agreement", "msa"],
>         "dest": "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Proposals / Quotes / Offers",
>         "contains": ["proposal", "quote", "offer"],
>         "dest": "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Immigration / Filings",
>         "contains": ["immigration", "i-589", "i589", "i-360", "i360", "i-130", "i130"],
>         "dest": "50_casework/60_filings",
>     },
> ]
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === REGISTRY / QID LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def load_registry() -> dict[str, Any]:
>     if not REGISTRY_PATH.exists():
>         # create a blank registry
>         data = {
>             "version": 1,
>             "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>             "entries": [],
>         }
>         save_registry(data)
>         return data
>     with REGISTRY_PATH.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         return json.load(f)
> 
> 
> def save_registry(data: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
>     REGISTRY_PATH.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
> 
> 
> def registry_qids(data: dict[str, Any]) -> set[str]:
>     entries = data.get("entries", [])
>     return {e.get("qid") for e in entries if "qid" in e}
> 
> 
> def generate_qid_unique(registry: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
>     """Generate a unique QID not already in the registry."""
>     used = registry_qids(registry)
>     while True:
>         date_part = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d")
>         rand_part = "".join(secrets.choice("ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789") for _ in range(4))
>         qid = f"QCL-{date_part}-{rand_part}"
>         if qid not in used:
>             return qid
> 
> 
> def register_client_in_registry(
>     registry: dict[str, Any],
>     qid: str,
>     client_name: str,
>     client_code: str,
>     client_root: Path,
>     band: str | None = None,
> ) -> None:
>     entries = registry.setdefault("entries", [])
>     band_final = band.strip() if band else "unassigned"
>     entry = {
>         "qid": qid,
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "band": band_final,
>         "root_path": str(client_root),
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>     }
>     entries.append(entry)
>     save_registry(registry)
>     print(f"[+] Registered client in QID registry ({REGISTRY_PATH.name}): {qid} ({band_final})")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === UTILITY & CORE LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def prompt_input(prompt: str, default: str | None = None) -> str:
>     if default:
>         full = f"{prompt} [{default}]: "
>     else:
>         full = f"{prompt}: "
>     val = input(full).strip()
>     return val or (default or "")
> 
> 
> def ensure_folders(root: Path, folders: list[str]) -> None:
>     print("\n[+] Ensuring canonical folder structure exists...")
>     created = 0
>     for rel in folders:
>         target = root / rel
>         if not target.exists():
>             target.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>             created += 1
>             print(f"  + created: {rel}")
>         else:
>             print(f"  = exists : {rel}")
>     print(f"Done. {created} folder(s) created.\n")
> 
> 
> def safe_move(root: Path, src: Path, dest_rel: str) -> None:
>     """
>     Move src (file or dir) to root/dest_rel.
>     If root/dest_rel already exists, append __DUP{n} so nothing is overwritten.
>     """
>     dest = root / dest_rel
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix  # includes dot if file
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     rel_src = src.relative_to(root)
>     rel_dest = candidate.relative_to(root)
>     print(f"  -> moving: {rel_src}  ==>  {rel_dest}")
>     shutil.move(str(src), str(candidate))
> 
> 
> def write_client_meta(root: Path, client_name: str, client_code: str, qid: str, band: str | None = None) -> None:
>     meta = {
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "qid": qid,
>         "band": band or "unassigned",
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>         "root_path": str(root),
>     }
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if meta_path.exists():
>         # Do not overwrite; create DUP
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             candidate = root / f"client.meta__DUP{n}.json"
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 meta_path = candidate
>                 break
>             n += 1
>     with meta_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         json.dump(meta, f, indent=2)
>     print(f"[+] Wrote client meta: {meta_path.relative_to(root)}")
> 
> 
> def slug_from_name(name: str) -> str:
>     """Make a small code like c.bbr from 'Built By Rays Construction'."""
>     if not name.strip():
>         return "c.client"
>     words = [w for w in name.replace("_", " ").split() if w]
>     if not words:
>         return "c.client"
>     initials = "".join(w[0].lower() for w in words[:3])
>     return f"c.{initials}"
> 
> 
> def scaffold_kb_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     kb_root = root / "kb_site"
>     readme = kb_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Knowledge Base Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's portable KB site (e.g. Starlight, Docusaurus, etc.).
> 
> Recommended:
> - /kb_site/src or /kb_site/docs for content
> - Integrate with QiOS/QiNote pipelines for automated sync
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: kb_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def scaffold_marketing_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     mkt_root = root / "marketing_site"
>     readme = mkt_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Marketing Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's marketing website project.
> 
> Recommended:
> - Use your standard QiAlly marketing template (e.g. Vite/React/Astro)
> - Connect to domain + Cloudflare/hosting of choice
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: marketing_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def normalize_filename(filename: str) -> str:
>     """
>     Apply a simple, predictable normalization:
>     - lowercase
>     - spaces & contiguous separators -> single '-'
>     - strip weird characters except alnum, '-', '_', '.'
>     """
>     p = Path(filename)
>     stem = p.stem.lower()
>     ext = p.suffix
> 
>     # Replace spaces and some punctuation with dash
>     stem = re.sub(r"[ \t]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"[\\/]+", "-", stem)
>     # Keep alnum, dash, underscore; drop others
>     stem = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\-_]+", "-", stem)
>     # Collapse multiple dashes
>     stem = re.sub(r"-{2,}", "-", stem).strip("-")
> 
>     return stem + ext
> 
> 
> # ===========================================
> # === INTERACTIVE REORGANIZATION (LEGACY) ====
> # ===========================================
> 
> def interactive_reorganize_move_rules(root: Path) -> None:
>     print("[*] Stage 1: Legacy MOVE_RULES (exact root names).")
>     print("    I will NOT delete or overwrite anything.\n")
> 
>     for src_name, dest_rel in MOVE_RULES.items():
>         src = root / src_name
>         if not src.exists():
>             continue
> 
>         print(f"Found: {src_name}/  ->  proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>         choice = input("  Move this now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>         if choice == "y":
>             safe_move(root, src, dest_rel)
>         else:
>             print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Stage 1 (MOVE_RULES) completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize_patterns(root: Path, use_normalization: bool) -> None:
>     print("[*] Stage 2: Pattern-based organization (file/folder name patterns).")
>     print("    Scanning for non-canonical items that match pattern rules.\n")
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     canonical_roots = {Path(f).parts[0] for f in folders if f}
> 
>     # Things we NEVER touch
>     ignore_names = {
>         "client.meta.json",
>         "client.meta__DUP.json",
>         REGISTRY_PATH.name,
>         Path(__file__).name,
>     }
> 
>     # Walk the tree
>     for path in sorted(root.rglob("*")):
>         if path.is_dir() and path == root:
>             continue
> 
>         rel = path.relative_to(root)
>         rel_parts = rel.parts
> 
>         # Skip anything already under canonical roots or _system
>         if rel_parts and (rel_parts[0] in canonical_roots or rel_parts[0] == "_system"):
>             continue
> 
>         if path.name in ignore_names:
>             continue
> 
>         name_lower = path.name.lower()
> 
>         for rule in PATTERN_RULES:
>             if any(substr in name_lower for substr in rule["contains"]):
>                 dest_dir = rule["dest"]
>                 label = rule.get("label", dest_dir)
>                 print(f"Pattern match [{label}]: {rel}")
>                 dest_display = dest_dir
> 
>                 # Build target path
>                 if path.is_file():
>                     new_name = normalize_filename(path.name) if use_normalization else path.name
>                     dest_rel = str(Path(dest_dir) / new_name)
>                 else:
>                     # For directories, don't rename automatically
>                     dest_rel = str(Path(dest_dir) / path.name)
> 
>                 print(f"  Proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>                 choice = input("  Move this item now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>                 if choice == "y":
>                     safe_move(root, path, dest_rel)
>                 else:
>                     print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>                 # Once matched by one rule, don't process further rules for this item
>                 break
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Stage 2 (PATTERN_RULES) completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize(root: Path) -> None:
>     # Stage 1: explicit MOVE_RULES
>     interactive_reorganize_move_rules(root)
> 
>     # Ask about filename normalization for pattern moves
>     norm_choice = input("Enable filename normalization for pattern-based moves? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>     use_normalization = norm_choice == "y"
> 
>     # Stage 2: pattern rules
>     interactive_reorganize_patterns(root, use_normalization)
> 
>     print("[✓] Reorganization pass completed.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === MODES: NEW / CLEANUP  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def mode_new_client() -> None:
>     print("\n=== NEW CLIENT SETUP ===")
> 
>     default_base = str(Path.cwd())
>     base_input = prompt_input("Base directory to create client folder in", default_base)
>     base_path = Path(base_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not base_path.exists():
>         print(f"Base path does not exist, creating: {base_path}")
>         base_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     client_name = prompt_input("Client display name (e.g. 'Built By Rays Construction')", "")
>     if not client_name:
>         print("Client name is required. Aborting.")
>         return
> 
>     default_code = slug_from_name(client_name)
>     client_code = prompt_input("Client code/folder name (e.g. 'c.bbr')", default_code)
>     if not client_code:
>         client_code = default_code
> 
>     band = prompt_input("Client band (e.g. 'gold', 'silver', 'standard')", "standard")
> 
>     # Resolve client root, avoid overwriting existing folder
>     client_root = base_path / client_code
>     if client_root.exists():
>         print(f"WARNING: {client_root} already exists.")
>         # Auto create a non-conflicting alternative
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             alt = base_path / f"{client_code}__NEW{n}"
>             if not alt.exists():
>                 client_root = alt
>                 print(f"Using new folder instead: {client_root}")
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     client_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     # Registry + QID
>     registry = load_registry()
>     qid = generate_qid_unique(registry)
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Creating client repo at: {client_root}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Name : {client_name}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Code : {client_code}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Band : {band}")
>     print(f"[+] QID         : {qid}\n")
> 
>     # Create structure
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(client_root, folders)
> 
>     # Meta + registry + scaffolds
>     write_client_meta(client_root, client_name, client_code, qid, band)
>     register_client_in_registry(registry, qid, client_name, client_code, client_root, band)
>     scaffold_kb_site(client_root)
>     scaffold_marketing_site(client_root)
> 
>     # Basic README at root if missing
>     readme = client_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = f"""# {client_name} ({client_code})
> 
> - QID: {qid}
> - Band: {band or 'standard'}
> - Created: {datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}Z
> 
> This is the portable QiAlly-style client workspace.
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: README.md")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] New client repo created.\n")
> 
> 
> def maybe_backfill_registry_from_meta(root: Path) -> None:
>     """
>     If the client root has client.meta.json but QID is missing from registry,
>     offer to backfill the registry.
>     """
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if not meta_path.exists():
>         return
> 
>     try:
>         with meta_path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>             meta = json.load(f)
>     except Exception:
>         return
> 
>     qid = meta.get("qid")
>     if not qid:
>         return
> 
>     registry = load_registry()
>     if qid in registry_qids(registry):
>         return  # already registered
> 
>     print(f"[!] client.meta.json found with QID {qid}, not in registry.")
>     choice = input("    Add this client to QID registry now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>     if choice != "y":
>         print("    Skipped registry backfill.\n")
>         return
> 
>     client_name = meta.get("client_name", "Unknown Client")
>     client_code = meta.get("client_code", "c.unknown")
>     band = meta.get("band", "unassigned")
>     register_client_in_registry(registry, qid, client_name, client_code, root, band)
>     print("    Registry backfilled from client.meta.json.\n")
> 
> 
> def mode_cleanup() -> None:
>     print("\n=== CLEAN UP EXISTING CLIENT FOLDERS ===")
> 
>     default_root = str(Path.cwd())
>     root_input = prompt_input("Existing client root path", default_root)
>     root = Path(root_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not root.exists():
>         print(f"ERROR: Path does not exist: {root}")
>         return
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Operating on: {root}\n")
> 
>     # Optional registry backfill
>     maybe_backfill_registry_from_meta(root)
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(root, folders)
>     interactive_reorganize(root)
> 
>     print("[✓] Cleanup done.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === ENTRYPOINT / MENU     ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def main() -> None:
>     print("=== QiAlly Client Spawner ===")
>     print("This tool can either:")
>     print("  1) Create a NEW client repo (portable structure + QID + registry)")
>     print("  2) Clean up / reorganize an EXISTING client repo\n")
> 
>     while True:
>         choice = prompt_input("Choose mode: [1] New client, [2] Cleanup, [Q] Quit", "1").lower()
>         if choice in ("1", "new", "n"):
>             mode_new_client()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("2", "cleanup", "c"):
>             mode_cleanup()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("q", "quit", "exit"):
>             print("Bye.")
>             return
>         else:
>             print("Invalid choice, try again.\n")
> 
> 
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>     main()
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> If you want, next pass we can:
> 
> - Add **bands with enforced enum** (`gold/silver/bronze/internal/pro-bono`)  
> - Add a `mode: registry` to list all clients / search by QID  
> - Add a `--noninteractive` flag so you can batch-convert a bunch of old client folders with one run.

### User
> maybe we need to have a template repo the spawner can use to copy over kb articles and other tempaltes so we can make the code is self lean as it can git clone this repo for all the resources its giong to need.

### Assistant
> Yup, you’re thinking correctly: **stop baking templates into the script** and let it **pull from a canonical template repo**.
> 
> Below is an updated `client_spawner.py` that:
> 
> - Still does:
>   - QID registry
>   - New client vs cleanup modes
>   - MOVE_RULES + PATTERN_RULES
>   - Filename normalization
> - **New:**
>   - **Template repo config block** (easy to edit)
>   - `git clone` / `git pull` a **client template repo** once into a local cache
>   - Copies template resources into each new client:
>     - KB starter content
>     - KB vault starter structure
>     - System templates, SOPs, etc.
>   - Uses **safe copy** (no overwrites; `__DUP#` if needed)
> 
> You’ll just point it at your **Qi client template** repo when you have it.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## How the template repo works (concept)
> 
> In your GitHub (or wherever), create something like:  
> `qiallyme/qi-client-template`
> 
> With structure for reusable stuff, for example:
> 
> ```text
> template_root/
> ├── kb_site/                 # Starter KB site skeleton
> ├── marketing_site/          # Starter marketing site skeleton
> ├── system_templates/        # Email, document, process templates
> ├── kb_vault_seed/           # Seed KB content
> └── README.md
> ```
> 
> The script will:
> 
> - Clone that into `SCRIPT_DIR / "_client_template"` (by default).
> - On each **New client**:
>   - Ask: use template repo?  
>   - If yes, it copies:
>     - `_client_template/kb_site` → `<client>/kb_site`
>     - `_client_template/marketing_site` → `<client>/marketing_site`
>     - `_client_template/system_templates` → `<client>/_system/templates`
>     - `_client_template/kb_vault_seed` → `<client>/60_resources/kb_vault`
> 
> You can tweak those mappings.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Updated `client_spawner.py`
> 
> Replace your existing one with this version:
> 
> ```python
> #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> QiAlly Client Spawner / Organizer
> 
> Modes:
>   - NEW CLIENT: create a portable client repo with standard structure,
>                 client meta (QID), kb_site stub, marketing_site stub,
>                 optional template repo content, and register in a global QID registry.
>   - CLEANUP:    reorganize an existing client folder to match the manifest,
>                 moving legacy folders into the new structure without overwriting,
>                 plus optional pattern-based moves and filename normalization.
> 
> This script is designed to live anywhere; it will ask you
> for base/client paths interactively.
> """
> 
> import json
> import shutil
> import secrets
> import re
> import subprocess
> from datetime import datetime
> from pathlib import Path
> from typing import Any
> 
> 
> SCRIPT_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
> REGISTRY_PATH = SCRIPT_DIR / "qid_registry.json"
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === TEMPLATE REPO CONFIG (EDIT THIS SECTION AS NEEDED)  ====
> # ============================================================
> # URL of the Git repo that contains your reusable client templates
> # (kb articles, kb site skeleton, marketing site skeleton, SOPs, etc.)
> TEMPLATE_REPO_URL = "https://github.com/your-org/qi-client-template.git"  # <-- EDIT THIS
> TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR = SCRIPT_DIR / "_client_template"
> 
> # How to map template subfolders into a new client repo.
> # Keys = paths inside TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR
> # Values = destination paths inside the client root.
> TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS = {
>     "kb_site": "kb_site",
>     "marketing_site": "marketing_site",
>     "system_templates": "_system/templates",
>     "kb_vault_seed": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === CLIENT FOLDER MANIFEST (EDIT THIS SECTION AS NEEDED) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> CLIENT_MANIFEST = {
>     "version": 1,
>     "description": "Canonical QiAlly client repo structure (portable, c.* style).",
>     "folders": [
>         # Internal/system
>         "_system",
>         "_system/logs",
>         "_system/templates",
>         "_system/tools",
>         "_system/workers",
>         "_system/scripts",
>         "_system/legacy",
> 
>         # Client profile
>         "10_profile",
>         "10_profile/30_ids-and-documents",
> 
>         # Engagement + agreements
>         "20_engagement",
>         "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>         "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>         "20_engagement/30_scope",
>         "20_engagement/40_policies",
>         "20_engagement/50_expectations",
>         "20_engagement/60_agreements",
> 
>         # Operations
>         "30_operations",
>         "30_operations/10_onboarding",
>         "30_operations/20_checklists",
>         "30_operations/30_access-credentials",
>         "30_operations/40_project-notes",
> 
>         # Finance
>         "40_finance",
>         "40_finance/10_invoices",
>         "40_finance/20_expenses",
>         "40_finance/30_bank",
>         "40_finance/40_assets",
>         "40_finance/50_tax",
>         "40_finance/60_reports",
> 
>         # Casework (e.g. immigration, audits, complex matters)
>         "50_casework",
>         "50_casework/10_overview",
>         "50_casework/20_bio-and-ids",
>         "50_casework/30_employment",
>         "50_casework/40_financial",
>         "50_casework/50_evidence",
>         "50_casework/60_filings",
> 
>         # Resources / KB
>         "60_resources",
>         "60_resources/guides",
>         "60_resources/training",
>         "60_resources/legal",
>         "60_resources/marketing",
>         "60_resources/media",
>         "60_resources/references",
>         "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>         # Archive
>         "70_archive",
> 
>         # Sites / projects
>         "kb_site",
>         "marketing_site",
>     ],
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === LEGACY MOVE RULES (EXACT TOP-LEVEL NAME -> NEW PATH) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> MOVE_RULES = {
>     # Legacy assets & intake
>     "_assets": "60_resources/media/_assets",
>     "_intake": "30_operations/10_onboarding/_intake",
> 
>     # Knowledge base vault (old location)
>     "kb_vault": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>     # Dev / system-y stuff -> _system
>     "apps": "_system/legacy/apps",
>     "components": "_system/legacy/components",
>     "data": "_system/legacy/data",
>     "docs": "_system/legacy/docs",
>     "logs": "_system/logs",
>     "projects": "_system/legacy/projects",
>     "sites": "_system/legacy/sites",
>     "templates": "_system/templates",
>     "tools": "_system/tools",
>     "workers": "_system/workers",
> 
>     # Example legacy categories
>     "brand": "60_resources/marketing/brand",
>     "finance": "40_finance/60_reports/finance_legacy",
>     "resources": "60_resources/references/resources_legacy",
>     "tech": "_system/legacy/tech",
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === PATTERN-BASED RULES (FUZZY MATCH -> DEST FOLDER) =======
> # ============================================================
> 
> PATTERN_RULES = [
>     {
>         "label": "Invoices",
>         "contains": ["invoice", "inv_"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/10_invoices",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Receipts & Expenses",
>         "contains": ["receipt", "receipts", "expense"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/20_expenses",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Tax",
>         "contains": ["tax", "1040", "schedule_c", "schc", "sch_c"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/50_tax",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Contracts / Agreements",
>         "contains": ["contract", "agreement", "msa"],
>         "dest": "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Proposals / Quotes / Offers",
>         "contains": ["proposal", "quote", "offer"],
>         "dest": "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Immigration / Filings",
>         "contains": ["immigration", "i-589", "i589", "i-360", "i360", "i-130", "i130"],
>         "dest": "50_casework/60_filings",
>     },
> ]
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === REGISTRY / QID LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def load_registry() -> dict[str, Any]:
>     if not REGISTRY_PATH.exists():
>         data = {
>             "version": 1,
>             "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>             "entries": [],
>         }
>         save_registry(data)
>         return data
>     with REGISTRY_PATH.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         return json.load(f)
> 
> 
> def save_registry(data: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
>     REGISTRY_PATH.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
> 
> 
> def registry_qids(data: dict[str, Any]) -> set[str]:
>     entries = data.get("entries", [])
>     return {e.get("qid") for e in entries if "qid" in e}
> 
> 
> def generate_qid_unique(registry: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
>     used = registry_qids(registry)
>     while True:
>         date_part = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d")
>         rand_part = "".join(secrets.choice("ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789") for _ in range(4))
>         qid = f"QCL-{date_part}-{rand_part}"
>         if qid not in used:
>             return qid
> 
> 
> def register_client_in_registry(
>     registry: dict[str, Any],
>     qid: str,
>     client_name: str,
>     client_code: str,
>     client_root: Path,
>     band: str | None = None,
> ) -> None:
>     entries = registry.setdefault("entries", [])
>     band_final = band.strip() if band else "unassigned"
>     entry = {
>         "qid": qid,
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "band": band_final,
>         "root_path": str(client_root),
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>     }
>     entries.append(entry)
>     save_registry(registry)
>     print(f"[+] Registered client in QID registry ({REGISTRY_PATH.name}): {qid} ({band_final})")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === UTILITY & CORE LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def prompt_input(prompt: str, default: str | None = None) -> str:
>     if default:
>         full = f"{prompt} [{default}]: "
>     else:
>         full = f"{prompt}: "
>     val = input(full).strip()
>     return val or (default or "")
> 
> 
> def ensure_folders(root: Path, folders: list[str]) -> None:
>     print("\n[+] Ensuring canonical folder structure exists...")
>     created = 0
>     for rel in folders:
>         target = root / rel
>         if not target.exists():
>             target.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>             created += 1
>             print(f"  + created: {rel}")
>         else:
>             print(f"  = exists : {rel}")
>     print(f"Done. {created} folder(s) created.\n")
> 
> 
> def safe_move(root: Path, src: Path, dest_rel: str) -> None:
>     dest = root / dest_rel
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     rel_src = src.relative_to(root)
>     rel_dest = candidate.relative_to(root)
>     print(f"  -> moving: {rel_src}  ==>  {rel_dest}")
>     shutil.move(str(src), str(candidate))
> 
> 
> def safe_copy(src: Path, dest: Path) -> None:
>     """
>     Copy src (file) to dest path. If dest exists, append __DUP{n} before extension.
>     """
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     shutil.copy2(src, candidate)
> 
> 
> def write_client_meta(root: Path, client_name: str, client_code: str, qid: str, band: str | None = None) -> None:
>     meta = {
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "qid": qid,
>         "band": band or "unassigned",
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>         "root_path": str(root),
>     }
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if meta_path.exists():
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             candidate = root / f"client.meta__DUP{n}.json"
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 meta_path = candidate
>                 break
>             n += 1
>     with meta_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         json.dump(meta, f, indent=2)
>     print(f"[+] Wrote client meta: {meta_path.relative_to(root)}")
> 
> 
> def slug_from_name(name: str) -> str:
>     if not name.strip():
>         return "c.client"
>     words = [w for w in name.replace("_", " ").split() if w]
>     if not words:
>         return "c.client"
>     initials = "".join(w[0].lower() for w in words[:3])
>     return f"c.{initials}"
> 
> 
> def scaffold_kb_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     kb_root = root / "kb_site"
>     readme = kb_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Knowledge Base Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's portable KB site (e.g. Starlight, Docusaurus, etc.).
> 
> Recommended:
> - /kb_site/src or /kb_site/docs for content
> - Integrate with QiOS/QiNote pipelines for automated sync
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: kb_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def scaffold_marketing_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     mkt_root = root / "marketing_site"
>     readme = mkt_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Marketing Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's marketing website project.
> 
> Recommended:
> - Use your standard QiAlly marketing template (e.g. Vite/React/Astro)
> - Connect to domain + Cloudflare/hosting of choice
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: marketing_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def normalize_filename(filename: str) -> str:
>     p = Path(filename)
>     stem = p.stem.lower()
>     ext = p.suffix
> 
>     stem = re.sub(r"[ \t]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"[\\/]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\-_]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"-{2,}", "-", stem).strip("-")
> 
>     return stem + ext
> 
> 
> # ====================================
> # === TEMPLATE REPO SUPPORT       ====
> # ====================================
> 
> def ensure_template_repo() -> bool:
>     """
>     Make sure TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR exists and is up to date.
>     Returns True if ready to use, False otherwise.
>     """
>     if not TEMPLATE_REPO_URL or TEMPLATE_REPO_URL.startswith("https://github.com/your-org"):
>         print("[!] TEMPLATE_REPO_URL is not configured. Skipping template clone.")
>         return False
> 
>     if TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR.exists():
>         # Try git pull
>         print(f"[*] Updating template repo at {TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR} (git pull)...")
>         try:
>             subprocess.run(
>                 ["git", "-C", str(TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR), "pull"],
>                 check=False,
>                 stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
>                 stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
>                 text=True,
>             )
>             print("[+] Template repo updated (or already up to date).")
>             return True
>         except Exception as e:
>             print(f"[!] Failed to pull template repo: {e}")
>             return False
>     else:
>         # Clone
>         print(f"[*] Cloning template repo from {TEMPLATE_REPO_URL} to {TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR}...")
>         try:
>             subprocess.run(
>                 ["git", "clone", TEMPLATE_REPO_URL, str(TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR)],
>                 check=True,
>             )
>             print("[+] Template repo cloned.")
>             return True
>         except Exception as e:
>             print(f"[!] Failed to clone template repo: {e}")
>             return False
> 
> 
> def copy_template_resources(client_root: Path) -> None:
>     """
>     Copy resources from TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR into the new client repo
>     according to TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS.
>     Never overwrites; uses safe_copy.
>     """
>     if not TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR.exists():
>         print("[!] Template repo directory does not exist; skipping template copy.")
>         return
> 
>     print("[*] Copying template resources into client repo...")
>     for src_rel, dest_rel in TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS.items():
>         src_dir = TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR / src_rel
>         if not src_dir.exists():
>             print(f"  - Template subfolder missing, skipping: {src_rel}")
>             continue
> 
>         # Walk all files
>         for path in src_dir.rglob("*"):
>             if path.is_dir():
>                 continue
>             # Avoid copying git metadata
>             if ".git" in path.parts:
>                 continue
> 
>             rel_from_src = path.relative_to(src_dir)
>             dest_path = client_root / dest_rel / rel_from_src
>             safe_copy(path, dest_path)
>             print(f"  + copied: {src_rel}/{rel_from_src} -> {dest_rel}/{rel_from_src}")
>     print("[✓] Template resources copied.\n")
> 
> 
> # ===========================================
> # === INTERACTIVE REORGANIZATION (LEGACY) ====
> # ===========================================
> 
> def interactive_reorganize_move_rules(root: Path) -> None:
>     print("[*] Stage 1: Legacy MOVE_RULES (exact root names).")
>     print("    I will NOT delete or overwrite anything.\n")
> 
>     for src_name, dest_rel in MOVE_RULES.items():
>         src = root / src_name
>         if not src.exists():
>             continue
> 
>         print(f"Found: {src_name}/  ->  proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>         choice = input("  Move this now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>         if choice == "y":
>             safe_move(root, src, dest_rel)
>         else:
>             print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Stage 1 (MOVE_RULES) completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize_patterns(root: Path, use_normalization: bool) -> None:
>     print("[*] Stage 2: Pattern-based organization (file/folder name patterns).")
>     print("    Scanning for non-canonical items that match pattern rules.\n")
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     canonical_roots = {Path(f).parts[0] for f in folders if f}
> 
>     ignore_names = {
>         "client.meta.json",
>         REGISTRY_PATH.name,
>         Path(__file__).name,
>     }
> 
>     for path in sorted(root.rglob("*")):
>         if path.is_dir() and path == root:
>             continue
> 
>         rel = path.relative_to(root)
>         rel_parts = rel.parts
> 
>         if rel_parts and (rel_parts[0] in canonical_roots or rel_parts[0] == "_system"):
>             continue
> 
>         if path.name in ignore_names:
>             continue
> 
>         name_lower = path.name.lower()
> 
>         for rule in PATTERN_RULES:
>             if any(substr in name_lower for substr in rule["contains"]):
>                 dest_dir = rule["dest"]
>                 label = rule.get("label", dest_dir)
>                 print(f"Pattern match [{label}]: {rel}")
> 
>                 if path.is_file():
>                     new_name = normalize_filename(path.name) if use_normalization else path.name
>                     dest_rel = str(Path(dest_dir) / new_name)
>                 else:
>                     dest_rel = str(Path(dest_dir) / path.name)
> 
>                 print(f"  Proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>                 choice = input("  Move this item now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>                 if choice == "y":
>                     safe_move(root, path, dest_rel)
>                 else:
>                     print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>                 break
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Stage 2 (PATTERN_RULES) completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize(root: Path) -> None:
>     interactive_reorganize_move_rules(root)
> 
>     norm_choice = input("Enable filename normalization for pattern-based moves? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>     use_normalization = norm_choice == "y"
> 
>     interactive_reorganize_patterns(root, use_normalization)
> 
>     print("[✓] Reorganization pass completed.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === MODES: NEW / CLEANUP  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def mode_new_client() -> None:
>     print("\n=== NEW CLIENT SETUP ===")
> 
>     default_base = str(Path.cwd())
>     base_input = prompt_input("Base directory to create client folder in", default_base)
>     base_path = Path(base_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not base_path.exists():
>         print(f"Base path does not exist, creating: {base_path}")
>         base_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     client_name = prompt_input("Client display name (e.g. 'Built By Rays Construction')", "")
>     if not client_name:
>         print("Client name is required. Aborting.")
>         return
> 
>     default_code = slug_from_name(client_name)
>     client_code = prompt_input("Client code/folder name (e.g. 'c.bbr')", default_code)
>     if not client_code:
>         client_code = default_code
> 
>     band = prompt_input("Client band (e.g. 'gold', 'silver', 'standard')", "standard")
> 
>     client_root = base_path / client_code
>     if client_root.exists():
>         print(f"WARNING: {client_root} already exists.")
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             alt = base_path / f"{client_code}__NEW{n}"
>             if not alt.exists():
>                 client_root = alt
>                 print(f"Using new folder instead: {client_root}")
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     client_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     registry = load_registry()
>     qid = generate_qid_unique(registry)
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Creating client repo at: {client_root}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Name : {client_name}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Code : {client_code}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Band : {band}")
>     print(f"[+] QID         : {qid}\n")
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(client_root, folders)
> 
>     write_client_meta(client_root, client_name, client_code, qid, band)
>     register_client_in_registry(registry, qid, client_name, client_code, client_root, band)
> 
>     # Optional template repo usage
>     use_templates = prompt_input("Pull/copy template repo resources into this client? [Y/n]", "y").lower()
>     if use_templates in ("y", "yes", ""):
>         if ensure_template_repo():
>             copy_template_resources(client_root)
>         else:
>             print("[!] Template repo not available; continuing without template content.\n")
> 
>     # Minimal scaffolds (only fill in if template repo didn't already give you something)
>     scaffold_kb_site(client_root)
>     scaffold_marketing_site(client_root)
> 
>     readme = client_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = f"""# {client_name} ({client_code})
> 
> - QID: {qid}
> - Band: {band or 'standard'}
> - Created: {datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}Z
> 
> This is the portable QiAlly-style client workspace.
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: README.md")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] New client repo created.\n")
> 
> 
> def maybe_backfill_registry_from_meta(root: Path) -> None:
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if not meta_path.exists():
>         return
> 
>     try:
>         with meta_path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>             meta = json.load(f)
>     except Exception:
>         return
> 
>     qid = meta.get("qid")
>     if not qid:
>         return
> 
>     registry = load_registry()
>     if qid in registry_qids(registry):
>         return
> 
>     print(f"[!] client.meta.json found with QID {qid}, not in registry.")
>     choice = input("    Add this client to QID registry now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>     if choice != "y":
>         print("    Skipped registry backfill.\n")
>         return
> 
>     client_name = meta.get("client_name", "Unknown Client")
>     client_code = meta.get("client_code", "c.unknown")
>     band = meta.get("band", "unassigned")
>     register_client_in_registry(registry, qid, client_name, client_code, root, band)
>     print("    Registry backfilled from client.meta.json.\n")
> 
> 
> def mode_cleanup() -> None:
>     print("\n=== CLEAN UP EXISTING CLIENT FOLDERS ===")
> 
>     default_root = str(Path.cwd())
>     root_input = prompt_input("Existing client root path", default_root)
>     root = Path(root_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not root.exists():
>         print(f"ERROR: Path does not exist: {root}")
>         return
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Operating on: {root}\n")
> 
>     maybe_backfill_registry_from_meta(root)
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(root, folders)
>     interactive_reorganize(root)
> 
>     print("[✓] Cleanup done.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === ENTRYPOINT / MENU     ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def main() -> None:
>     print("=== QiAlly Client Spawner ===")
>     print("This tool can either:")
>     print("  1) Create a NEW client repo (portable structure + QID + registry + templates)")
>     print("  2) Clean up / reorganize an EXISTING client repo\n")
> 
>     while True:
>         choice = prompt_input("Choose mode: [1] New client, [2] Cleanup, [Q] Quit", "1").lower()
>         if choice in ("1", "new", "n"):
>             mode_new_client()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("2", "cleanup", "c"):
>             mode_cleanup()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("q", "quit", "exit"):
>             print("Bye.")
>             return
>         else:
>             print("Invalid choice, try again.\n")
> 
> 
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>     main()
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> ### What you need to do on your side
> 
> 1. **Create the template repo** with whatever structure you want:
>    - `kb_site/`
>    - `marketing_site/`
>    - `system_templates/`
>    - `kb_vault_seed/`
> 2. Update:
>    - `TEMPLATE_REPO_URL`
>    - `TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS` if your template folders are named differently.
> 3. Run:
> 
> ```bash
> python client_spawner.py
> ```
> 
> Choose **New client**, let it use the template repo, and you’ve now got:
> 
> - Standard folder skeleton
> - QID + registry
> - KB + marketing starter
