> - All mapped, consistent, and portable.
> 
> If you want, next step we can define **band rules** (e.g. gold gets more template modules, bronze gets minimal) or add a **“registry view” mode** to list/search clients.

### User
> the registry probably needs to live on the repo too and the spawner can update the registry. https://github.com/qiallyme/qi-client-template.git

### Assistant
> Good catch. Easiest way: **the registry lives in the same repo as the spawner** (which *is* a Git repo), and the spawner updates it. You then just `git add/commit/push` like anything else.
> 
> You also gave the real template repo:
> 
> > `https://github.com/qiallyme/qi-client-template.git`
> 
> So we’ll wire that in.
> 
> Below is an updated **`client_spawner.py`** that:
> 
> - Keeps **QID registry** in the same repo as the script  
>   - `REGISTRY_PATH = SCRIPT_DIR / "qi_client_registry.json"`
>   - Under Git with everything else
> - Uses your **template repo** URL:
>   - `TEMPLATE_REPO_URL = "https://github.com/qiallyme/qi-client-template.git"`
> - Still:
>   - Creates new client repos with QID, band, meta file
>   - Maintains global registry
>   - Clones/pulls the template repo into `_client_template/`
>   - Copies mapped template folders into each new client
>   - Has MOVE_RULES, PATTERN_RULES, normalization, cleanup mode
> 
> You can drop this script directly into the **qi-client-template** repo (or a dedicated ops repo). The registry file will sit next to it and be tracked by Git.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### Updated `client_spawner.py`
> 
> ```python
> #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> QiAlly Client Spawner / Organizer
> 
> Modes:
>   - NEW CLIENT: create a portable client repo with standard structure,
>                 client meta (QID), kb_site stub, marketing_site stub,
>                 optional template repo content, and register in a global QID registry.
>   - CLEANUP:    reorganize an existing client folder to match the manifest,
>                 moving legacy folders into the new structure without overwriting,
>                 plus optional pattern-based moves and filename normalization.
> 
> INTENDED SETUP:
> - Put this script in your ops / template repo (e.g. qi-client-template).
> - The QID registry file (qi_client_registry.json) lives in the same repo
>   and should be committed to Git so your registry is versioned.
> """
> 
> import json
> import shutil
> import secrets
> import re
> import subprocess
> from datetime import datetime
> from pathlib import Path
> from typing import Any
> 
> 
> SCRIPT_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
> 
> # Global QID registry lives in the SAME repo as this script, and is git-tracked.
> REGISTRY_PATH = SCRIPT_DIR / "qi_client_registry.json"
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === TEMPLATE REPO CONFIG (EDIT ONLY IF YOU CHANGE URL)  ====
> # ============================================================
> # Central template repo for KB + marketing seeds, etc.
> TEMPLATE_REPO_URL = "https://github.com/qiallyme/qi-client-template.git"
> TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR = SCRIPT_DIR / "_client_template"
> 
> # How to map template subfolders into a new client repo.
> # Keys = paths inside TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR
> # Values = destination paths inside the client root.
> TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS = {
>     "kb_site": "kb_site",
>     "marketing_site": "marketing_site",
>     "system_templates": "_system/templates",
>     "kb_vault_seed": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === CLIENT FOLDER MANIFEST (EDIT THIS SECTION AS NEEDED) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> CLIENT_MANIFEST = {
>     "version": 1,
>     "description": "Canonical QiAlly client repo structure (portable, c.* style).",
>     "folders": [
>         # Internal/system
>         "_system",
>         "_system/logs",
>         "_system/templates",
>         "_system/tools",
>         "_system/workers",
>         "_system/scripts",
>         "_system/legacy",
> 
>         # Client profile
>         "10_profile",
>         "10_profile/30_ids-and-documents",
> 
>         # Engagement + agreements
>         "20_engagement",
>         "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>         "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>         "20_engagement/30_scope",
>         "20_engagement/40_policies",
>         "20_engagement/50_expectations",
>         "20_engagement/60_agreements",
> 
>         # Operations
>         "30_operations",
>         "30_operations/10_onboarding",
>         "30_operations/20_checklists",
>         "30_operations/30_access-credentials",
>         "30_operations/40_project-notes",
> 
>         # Finance
>         "40_finance",
>         "40_finance/10_invoices",
>         "40_finance/20_expenses",
>         "40_finance/30_bank",
>         "40_finance/40_assets",
>         "40_finance/50_tax",
>         "40_finance/60_reports",
> 
>         # Casework (e.g. immigration, audits, complex matters)
>         "50_casework",
>         "50_casework/10_overview",
>         "50_casework/20_bio-and-ids",
>         "50_casework/30_employment",
>         "50_casework/40_financial",
>         "50_casework/50_evidence",
>         "50_casework/60_filings",
> 
>         # Resources / KB
>         "60_resources",
>         "60_resources/guides",
>         "60_resources/training",
>         "60_resources/legal",
>         "60_resources/marketing",
>         "60_resources/media",
>         "60_resources/references",
>         "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>         # Archive
>         "70_archive",
> 
>         # Sites / projects
>         "kb_site",
>         "marketing_site",
>     ],
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === LEGACY MOVE RULES (EXACT TOP-LEVEL NAME -> NEW PATH) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> MOVE_RULES = {
>     # Legacy assets & intake
>     "_assets": "60_resources/media/_assets",
>     "_intake": "30_operations/10_onboarding/_intake",
> 
>     # Knowledge base vault (old location)
>     "kb_vault": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>     # Dev / system-y stuff -> _system
>     "apps": "_system/legacy/apps",
>     "components": "_system/legacy/components",
>     "data": "_system/legacy/data",
>     "docs": "_system/legacy/docs",
>     "logs": "_system/logs",
>     "projects": "_system/legacy/projects",
>     "sites": "_system/legacy/sites",
>     "templates": "_system/templates",
>     "tools": "_system/tools",
>     "workers": "_system/workers",
> 
>     # Example legacy categories
>     "brand": "60_resources/marketing/brand",
>     "finance": "40_finance/60_reports/finance_legacy",
>     "resources": "60_resources/references/resources_legacy",
>     "tech": "_system/legacy/tech",
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === PATTERN-BASED RULES (FUZZY MATCH -> DEST FOLDER) =======
> # ============================================================
> 
> PATTERN_RULES = [
>     {
>         "label": "Invoices",
>         "contains": ["invoice", "inv_"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/10_invoices",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Receipts & Expenses",
>         "contains": ["receipt", "receipts", "expense"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/20_expenses",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Tax",
>         "contains": ["tax", "1040", "schedule_c", "schc", "sch_c"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/50_tax",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Contracts / Agreements",
>         "contains": ["contract", "agreement", "msa"],
>         "dest": "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Proposals / Quotes / Offers",
>         "contains": ["proposal", "quote", "offer"],
>         "dest": "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Immigration / Filings",
>         "contains": ["immigration", "i-589", "i589", "i-360", "i360", "i-130", "i130"],
>         "dest": "50_casework/60_filings",
>     },
> ]
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === REGISTRY / QID LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def load_registry() -> dict[str, Any]:
>     if not REGISTRY_PATH.exists():
>         data = {
>             "version": 1,
>             "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>             "entries": [],
>         }
>         save_registry(data)
>         return data
>     with REGISTRY_PATH.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         return json.load(f)
> 
> 
> def save_registry(data: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
>     REGISTRY_PATH.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
> 
> 
> def registry_qids(data: dict[str, Any]) -> set[str]:
>     entries = data.get("entries", [])
>     return {e.get("qid") for e in entries if "qid" in e}
> 
> 
> def generate_qid_unique(registry: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
>     used = registry_qids(registry)
>     while True:
>         date_part = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d")
>         rand_part = "".join(secrets.choice("ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789") for _ in range(4))
>         qid = f"QCL-{date_part}-{rand_part}"
>         if qid not in used:
>             return qid
> 
> 
> def register_client_in_registry(
>     registry: dict[str, Any],
>     qid: str,
>     client_name: str,
>     client_code: str,
>     client_root: Path,
>     band: str | None = None,
> ) -> None:
>     entries = registry.setdefault("entries", [])
>     band_final = band.strip() if band else "unassigned"
>     entry = {
>         "qid": qid,
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "band": band_final,
>         "root_path": str(client_root),
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>     }
>     entries.append(entry)
>     save_registry(registry)
>     print(f"[+] Registered client in QID registry ({REGISTRY_PATH.name}): {qid} ({band_final})")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === UTILITY & CORE LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def prompt_input(prompt: str, default: str | None = None) -> str:
>     if default:
>         full = f"{prompt} [{default}]: "
>     else:
>         full = f"{prompt}: "
>     val = input(full).strip()
>     return val or (default or "")
> 
> 
> def ensure_folders(root: Path, folders: list[str]) -> None:
>     print("\n[+] Ensuring canonical folder structure exists...")
>     created = 0
>     for rel in folders:
>         target = root / rel
>         if not target.exists():
>             target.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>             created += 1
>             print(f"  + created: {rel}")
>         else:
>             print(f"  = exists : {rel}")
>     print(f"Done. {created} folder(s) created.\n")
> 
> 
> def safe_move(root: Path, src: Path, dest_rel: str) -> None:
>     dest = root / dest_rel
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     rel_src = src.relative_to(root)
>     rel_dest = candidate.relative_to(root)
>     print(f"  -> moving: {rel_src}  ==>  {rel_dest}")
>     shutil.move(str(src), str(candidate))
> 
> 
> def safe_copy(src: Path, dest: Path) -> None:
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     shutil.copy2(src, candidate)
> 
> 
> def write_client_meta(root: Path, client_name: str, client_code: str, qid: str, band: str | None = None) -> None:
>     meta = {
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "qid": qid,
>         "band": band or "unassigned",
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>         "root_path": str(root),
>     }
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if meta_path.exists():
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             candidate = root / f"client.meta__DUP{n}.json"
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 meta_path = candidate
>                 break
>             n += 1
>     with meta_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         json.dump(meta, f, indent=2)
>     print(f"[+] Wrote client meta: {meta_path.relative_to(root)}")
> 
> 
> def slug_from_name(name: str) -> str:
>     if not name.strip():
>         return "c.client"
>     words = [w for w in name.replace("_", " ").split() if w]
>     if not words:
>         return "c.client"
>     initials = "".join(w[0].lower() for w in words[:3])
>     return f"c.{initials}"
> 
> 
> def scaffold_kb_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     kb_root = root / "kb_site"
>     readme = kb_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Knowledge Base Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's portable KB site (e.g. Starlight, Docusaurus, etc.).
> 
> Recommended:
> - /kb_site/src or /kb_site/docs for content
> - Integrate with QiOS/QiNote pipelines for automated sync
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: kb_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def scaffold_marketing_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     mkt_root = root / "marketing_site"
>     readme = mkt_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Marketing Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's marketing website project.
> 
> Recommended:
> - Use your standard QiAlly marketing template (e.g. Vite/React/Astro)
> - Connect to domain + Cloudflare/hosting of choice
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: marketing_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def normalize_filename(filename: str) -> str:
>     p = Path(filename)
>     stem = p.stem.lower()
>     ext = p.suffix
> 
>     stem = re.sub(r"[ \t]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"[\\/]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\-_]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"-{2,}", "-", stem).strip("-")
> 
>     return stem + ext
> 
> 
> # ====================================
> # === TEMPLATE REPO SUPPORT       ====
> # ====================================
> 
> def ensure_template_repo() -> bool:
>     """
>     Make sure TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR exists and is up to date.
>     Returns True if ready to use, False otherwise.
>     """
>     if not TEMPLATE_REPO_URL:
>         print("[!] TEMPLATE_REPO_URL is not configured. Skipping template clone.")
>         return False
> 
>     if TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR.exists():
>         print(f"[*] Updating template repo at {TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR} (git pull)...")
>         try:
>             subprocess.run(
>                 ["git", "-C", str(TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR), "pull"],
>                 check=False,
>                 stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
>                 stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
>                 text=True,
>             )
>             print("[+] Template repo updated (or already up to date).")
>             return True
>         except Exception as e:
>             print(f"[!] Failed to pull template repo: {e}")
>             return False
>     else:
>         print(f"[*] Cloning template repo from {TEMPLATE_REPO_URL} to {TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR}...")
>         try:
>             subprocess.run(
>                 ["git", "clone", TEMPLATE_REPO_URL, str(TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR)],
>                 check=True,
>             )
>             print("[+] Template repo cloned.")
>             return True
>         except Exception as e:
>             print(f"[!] Failed to clone template repo: {e}")
>             return False
> 
> 
> def copy_template_resources(client_root: Path) -> None:
>     """
>     Copy resources from TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR into the new client repo
>     according to TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS.
>     Never overwrites; uses safe_copy.
>     """
>     if not TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR.exists():
>         print("[!] Template repo directory does not exist; skipping template copy.")
>         return
> 
>     print("[*] Copying template resources into client repo...")
>     for src_rel, dest_rel in TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS.items():
>         src_dir = TEMPLATE_LOCAL_DIR / src_rel
>         if not src_dir.exists():
>             print(f"  - Template subfolder missing, skipping: {src_rel}")
>             continue
> 
>         for path in src_dir.rglob("*"):
>             if path.is_dir():
>                 continue
>             if ".git" in path.parts:
>                 continue
> 
>             rel_from_src = path.relative_to(src_dir)
>             dest_path = client_root / dest_rel / rel_from_src
>             safe_copy(path, dest_path)
>             print(f"  + copied: {src_rel}/{rel_from_src} -> {dest_rel}/{rel_from_src}")
>     print("[✓] Template resources copied.\n")
> 
> 
> # ===========================================
> # === INTERACTIVE REORGANIZATION (LEGACY) ====
> # ===========================================
> 
> def interactive_reorganize_move_rules(root: Path) -> None:
>     print("[*] Stage 1: Legacy MOVE_RULES (exact root names).")
>     print("    I will NOT delete or overwrite anything.\n")
> 
>     for src_name, dest_rel in MOVE_RULES.items():
>         src = root / src_name
>         if not src.exists():
>             continue
> 
>         print(f"Found: {src_name}/  ->  proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>         choice = input("  Move this now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>         if choice == "y":
>             safe_move(root, src, dest_rel)
>         else:
>             print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Stage 1 (MOVE_RULES) completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize_patterns(root: Path, use_normalization: bool) -> None:
>     print("[*] Stage 2: Pattern-based organization (file/folder name patterns).")
>     print("    Scanning for non-canonical items that match pattern rules.\n")
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     canonical_roots = {Path(f).parts[0] for f in folders if f}
> 
>     ignore_names = {
>         "client.meta.json",
>         REGISTRY_PATH.name,
>         Path(__file__).name,
>     }
> 
>     for path in sorted(root.rglob("*")):
>         if path.is_dir() and path == root:
>             continue
> 
>         rel = path.relative_to(root)
>         rel_parts = rel.parts
> 
>         if rel_parts and (rel_parts[0] in canonical_roots or rel_parts[0] == "_system"):
>             continue
> 
>         if path.name in ignore_names:
>             continue
> 
>         name_lower = path.name.lower()
> 
>         for rule in PATTERN_RULES:
>             if any(substr in name_lower for substr in rule["contains"]):
>                 dest_dir = rule["dest"]
>                 label = rule.get("label", dest_dir)
>                 print(f"Pattern match [{label}]: {rel}")
> 
>                 if path.is_file():
>                     new_name = normalize_filename(path.name) if use_normalization else path.name
>                     dest_rel = str(Path(dest_dir) / new_name)
>                 else:
>                     dest_rel = str(Path(dest_dir) / path.name)
> 
>                 print(f"  Proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>                 choice = input("  Move this item now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>                 if choice == "y":
>                     safe_move(root, path, dest_rel)
>                 else:
>                     print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>                 break
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Stage 2 (PATTERN_RULES) completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize(root: Path) -> None:
>     interactive_reorganize_move_rules(root)
> 
>     norm_choice = input("Enable filename normalization for pattern-based moves? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>     use_normalization = norm_choice == "y"
> 
>     interactive_reorganize_patterns(root, use_normalization)
> 
>     print("[✓] Reorganization pass completed.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === MODES: NEW / CLEANUP  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def mode_new_client() -> None:
>     print("\n=== NEW CLIENT SETUP ===")
> 
>     default_base = str(Path.cwd())
>     base_input = prompt_input("Base directory to create client folder in", default_base)
>     base_path = Path(base_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not base_path.exists():
>         print(f"Base path does not exist, creating: {base_path}")
>         base_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     client_name = prompt_input("Client display name (e.g. 'Built By Rays Construction')", "")
>     if not client_name:
>         print("Client name is required. Aborting.")
>         return
> 
>     default_code = slug_from_name(client_name)
>     client_code = prompt_input("Client code/folder name (e.g. 'c.bbr')", default_code)
>     if not client_code:
>         client_code = default_code
> 
>     band = prompt_input("Client band (e.g. 'gold', 'silver', 'standard')", "standard")
> 
>     client_root = base_path / client_code
>     if client_root.exists():
>         print(f"WARNING: {client_root} already exists.")
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             alt = base_path / f"{client_code}__NEW{n}"
>             if not alt.exists():
>                 client_root = alt
>                 print(f"Using new folder instead: {client_root}")
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     client_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     registry = load_registry()
>     qid = generate_qid_unique(registry)
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Creating client repo at: {client_root}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Name : {client_name}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Code : {client_code}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Band : {band}")
>     print(f"[+] QID         : {qid}\n")
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(client_root, folders)
> 
>     write_client_meta(client_root, client_name, client_code, qid, band)
>     register_client_in_registry(registry, qid, client_name, client_code, client_root, band)
> 
>     use_templates = prompt_input("Pull/copy template repo resources into this client? [Y/n]", "y").lower()
>     if use_templates in ("y", "yes", ""):
>         if ensure_template_repo():
>             copy_template_resources(client_root)
>         else:
>             print("[!] Template repo not available; continuing without template content.\n")
> 
>     scaffold_kb_site(client_root)
>     scaffold_marketing_site(client_root)
> 
>     readme = client_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = f"""# {client_name} ({client_code})
> 
> - QID: {qid}
> - Band: {band or 'standard'}
> - Created: {datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}Z
> 
> This is the portable QiAlly-style client workspace.
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: README.md")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] New client repo created.\n")
> 
> 
> def maybe_backfill_registry_from_meta(root: Path) -> None:
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if not meta_path.exists():
>         return
> 
>     try:
>         with meta_path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>             meta = json.load(f)
>     except Exception:
>         return
> 
>     qid = meta.get("qid")
>     if not qid:
>         return
> 
>     registry = load_registry()
>     if qid in registry_qids(registry):
>         return
> 
>     print(f"[!] client.meta.json found with QID {qid}, not in registry.")
>     choice = input("    Add this client to QID registry now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>     if choice != "y":
>         print("    Skipped registry backfill.\n")
>         return
> 
>     client_name = meta.get("client_name", "Unknown Client")
>     client_code = meta.get("client_code", "c.unknown")
>     band = meta.get("band", "unassigned")
>     register_client_in_registry(registry, qid, client_name, client_code, root, band)
>     print("    Registry backfilled from client.meta.json.\n")
> 
> 
> def mode_cleanup() -> None:
>     print("\n=== CLEAN UP EXISTING CLIENT FOLDERS ===")
> 
>     default_root = str(Path.cwd())
>     root_input = prompt_input("Existing client root path", default_root)
>     root = Path(root_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not root.exists():
>         print(f"ERROR: Path does not exist: {root}")
>         return
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Operating on: {root}\n")
> 
>     maybe_backfill_registry_from_meta(root)
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(root, folders)
>     interactive_reorganize(root)
> 
>     print("[✓] Cleanup done.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === ENTRYPOINT / MENU     ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def main() -> None:
>     print("=== QiAlly Client Spawner ===")
>     print("This tool can either:")
>     print("  1) Create a NEW client repo (portable structure + QID + registry + templates)")
>     print("  2) Clean up / reorganize an EXISTING client repo\n")
> 
>     while True:
>         choice = prompt_input("Choose mode: [1] New client, [2] Cleanup, [Q] Quit", "1").lower()
>         if choice in ("1", "new", "n"):
>             mode_new_client()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("2", "cleanup", "c"):
>             mode_cleanup()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("q", "quit", "exit"):
>             print("Bye.")
>             return
>         else:
>             print("Invalid choice, try again.\n")
> 
> 
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>     main()
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> **How to wire it up cleanly:**
> 
> 1. Clone `qi-client-template` locally.
> 2. Drop this `client_spawner.py` into the repo root.
> 3. Run it from there:
> 
> ```bash
> cd qi-client-template
> python client_spawner.py
> ```
> 
> 4. The first time, it will create `qi_client_registry.json` in that repo.
> 5. When you add a client, it:
>    - updates `qi_client_registry.json`
>    - writes `client.meta.json` inside the client’s folder
> 6. You just `git add qi_client_registry.json client_spawner.py` etc. and commit.
> 
> If you want, next step we can add a **“registry viewer” mode** (list clients, filter by band, search by QID) so you can use this as your little CLI CRM.

### User
> the spawner should just live in the template repo you clone the repor client the start bash or something the spawner pulls up like hey we making a new client or fixing an old one logic, then depending on which one it ask the path to create the new client or the path of the old client to fix, so its litterally sitting in it resources that is can copy over to the new client or update the old client repo. but it never updates anything other than the registry in the template report to ensure its intake, I have to make update to the template repo manually.

### Assistant
> Got it. So:
> 
> - **Spawner lives in the template repo.**
> - You clone that **once**.
> - For each client, you run the spawner from that repo.
> - It:
>   - Asks: **new client or fix existing?**
>   - Asks for **external path** (new client location or existing client root).
>   - Copies resources **from the template repo into the client repo**.
>   - **Only file it ever writes in the template repo itself**: the **QID registry**.
>   - You update template content manually in the template repo.
> 
> Below is a cleaned, aligned version of `client_spawner.py` that does exactly that.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### Recommended template repo layout
> 
> In `qi-client-template` repo, you can do something like:
> 
> ```text
> qi-client-template/
> ├── client_spawner.py
> ├── qi_client_registry.json        # auto-managed by spawner
> └── templates/
>     ├── kb_site/                   # starter KB site skeleton
>     ├── marketing_site/            # starter marketing site skeleton
>     ├── system_templates/          # SOPs, docs, emails, etc.
>     └── kb_vault_seed/             # seed KB content
> ```
> 
> You’ll maintain everything under `templates/` manually.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### `client_spawner.py`
> 
> Drop this in the **root of `qi-client-template`**.
> 
> ```python
> #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> QiAlly Client Spawner / Organizer
> 
> LIVES IN: qi-client-template repo.
> 
> Behavior:
> - Asks: New client or Cleanup existing?
> - For NEW:
>     - Asks where to create the client folder (external path).
>     - Asks client name, client code, band.
>     - Generates QID, creates canonical structure.
>     - Copies template resources from THIS repo's /templates into the client.
>     - Writes client.meta.json inside the client folder.
>     - Updates qi_client_registry.json in THIS repo.
> - For CLEANUP:
>     - Asks for existing client root path.
>     - Ensures canonical folders.
>     - Offers to move legacy folders (MOVE_RULES).
>     - Offers pattern-based moves (PATTERN_RULES), with optional filename normalization.
>     - Only touches the client folder + registry (if backfilling); never template content.
> 
> The ONLY thing this script writes in the template repo:
>     - qi_client_registry.json
> """
> 
> import json
> import shutil
> import secrets
> import re
> from datetime import datetime
> from pathlib import Path
> from typing import Any
> 
> 
> SCRIPT_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
> 
> # Global QID registry lives in the SAME repo as this script, and is git-tracked.
> REGISTRY_PATH = SCRIPT_DIR / "qi_client_registry.json"
> 
> # Root where reusable templates live INSIDE the template repo.
> TEMPLATE_ROOT = SCRIPT_DIR / "templates"
> 
> # How to map template subfolders into a new client repo.
> # Keys = paths inside TEMPLATE_ROOT
> # Values = destination paths inside the client root.
> TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS = {
>     "kb_site": "kb_site",
>     "marketing_site": "marketing_site",
>     "system_templates": "_system/templates",
>     "kb_vault_seed": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === CLIENT FOLDER MANIFEST (EDIT THIS SECTION AS NEEDED) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> CLIENT_MANIFEST = {
>     "version": 1,
>     "description": "Canonical QiAlly client repo structure (portable, c.* style).",
>     "folders": [
>         # Internal/system
>         "_system",
>         "_system/logs",
>         "_system/templates",
>         "_system/tools",
>         "_system/workers",
>         "_system/scripts",
>         "_system/legacy",
> 
>         # Client profile
>         "10_profile",
>         "10_profile/30_ids-and-documents",
> 
>         # Engagement + agreements
>         "20_engagement",
>         "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>         "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>         "20_engagement/30_scope",
>         "20_engagement/40_policies",
>         "20_engagement/50_expectations",
>         "20_engagement/60_agreements",
> 
>         # Operations
>         "30_operations",
>         "30_operations/10_onboarding",
>         "30_operations/20_checklists",
>         "30_operations/30_access-credentials",
>         "30_operations/40_project-notes",
> 
>         # Finance
>         "40_finance",
>         "40_finance/10_invoices",
>         "40_finance/20_expenses",
>         "40_finance/30_bank",
>         "40_finance/40_assets",
>         "40_finance/50_tax",
>         "40_finance/60_reports",
> 
>         # Casework (e.g. immigration, audits, complex matters)
>         "50_casework",
>         "50_casework/10_overview",
>         "50_casework/20_bio-and-ids",
>         "50_casework/30_employment",
>         "50_casework/40_financial",
>         "50_casework/50_evidence",
>         "50_casework/60_filings",
> 
>         # Resources / KB
>         "60_resources",
>         "60_resources/guides",
>         "60_resources/training",
>         "60_resources/legal",
>         "60_resources/marketing",
>         "60_resources/media",
>         "60_resources/references",
>         "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>         # Archive
>         "70_archive",
> 
>         # Sites / projects
>         "kb_site",
>         "marketing_site",
>     ],
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === LEGACY MOVE RULES (EXACT TOP-LEVEL NAME -> NEW PATH) ===
> # ============================================================
> 
> MOVE_RULES = {
>     # Legacy assets & intake
>     "_assets": "60_resources/media/_assets",
>     "_intake": "30_operations/10_onboarding/_intake",
> 
>     # Knowledge base vault (old location)
>     "kb_vault": "60_resources/kb_vault",
> 
>     # Dev / system-y stuff -> _system
>     "apps": "_system/legacy/apps",
>     "components": "_system/legacy/components",
>     "data": "_system/legacy/data",
>     "docs": "_system/legacy/docs",
>     "logs": "_system/logs",
>     "projects": "_system/legacy/projects",
>     "sites": "_system/legacy/sites",
>     "templates": "_system/templates",
>     "tools": "_system/tools",
>     "workers": "_system/workers",
> 
>     # Example legacy categories
>     "brand": "60_resources/marketing/brand",
>     "finance": "40_finance/60_reports/finance_legacy",
>     "resources": "60_resources/references/resources_legacy",
>     "tech": "_system/legacy/tech",
> }
> 
> # ============================================================
> # === PATTERN-BASED RULES (FUZZY MATCH -> DEST FOLDER) =======
> # ============================================================
> 
> PATTERN_RULES = [
>     {
>         "label": "Invoices",
>         "contains": ["invoice", "inv_"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/10_invoices",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Receipts & Expenses",
>         "contains": ["receipt", "receipts", "expense"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/20_expenses",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Tax",
>         "contains": ["tax", "1040", "schedule_c", "schc", "sch_c"],
>         "dest": "40_finance/50_tax",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Contracts / Agreements",
>         "contains": ["contract", "agreement", "msa"],
>         "dest": "20_engagement/20_contracts",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Proposals / Quotes / Offers",
>         "contains": ["proposal", "quote", "offer"],
>         "dest": "20_engagement/10_proposals",
>     },
>     {
>         "label": "Immigration / Filings",
>         "contains": ["immigration", "i-589", "i589", "i-360", "i360", "i-130", "i130"],
>         "dest": "50_casework/60_filings",
>     },
> ]
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === REGISTRY / QID LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def load_registry() -> dict[str, Any]:
>     if not REGISTRY_PATH.exists():
>         data = {
>             "version": 1,
>             "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>             "entries": [],
>         }
>         save_registry(data)
>         return data
>     with REGISTRY_PATH.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         return json.load(f)
> 
> 
> def save_registry(data: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
>     REGISTRY_PATH.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
> 
> 
> def registry_qids(data: dict[str, Any]) -> set[str]:
>     entries = data.get("entries", [])
>     return {e.get("qid") for e in entries if "qid" in e}
> 
> 
> def generate_qid_unique(registry: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
>     used = registry_qids(registry)
>     while True:
>         date_part = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d")
>         rand_part = "".join(secrets.choice("ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789") for _ in range(4))
>         qid = f"QCL-{date_part}-{rand_part}"
>         if qid not in used:
>             return qid
> 
> 
> def register_client_in_registry(
>     registry: dict[str, Any],
>     qid: str,
>     client_name: str,
>     client_code: str,
>     client_root: Path,
>     band: str | None = None,
> ) -> None:
>     entries = registry.setdefault("entries", [])
>     band_final = band.strip() if band else "unassigned"
>     entry = {
>         "qid": qid,
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "band": band_final,
>         "root_path": str(client_root),
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>     }
>     entries.append(entry)
>     save_registry(registry)
>     print(f"[+] Registered client in QID registry ({REGISTRY_PATH.name}): {qid} ({band_final})")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === UTILITY & CORE LOGIC  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def prompt_input(prompt: str, default: str | None = None) -> str:
>     if default:
>         full = f"{prompt} [{default}]: "
>     else:
>         full = f"{prompt}: "
>     val = input(full).strip()
>     return val or (default or "")
> 
> 
> def ensure_folders(root: Path, folders: list[str]) -> None:
>     print("\n[+] Ensuring canonical folder structure exists...")
>     created = 0
>     for rel in folders:
>         target = root / rel
>         if not target.exists():
>             target.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>             created += 1
>             print(f"  + created: {rel}")
>         else:
>             print(f"  = exists : {rel}")
>     print(f"Done. {created} folder(s) created.\n")
> 
> 
> def safe_move(root: Path, src: Path, dest_rel: str) -> None:
>     dest = root / dest_rel
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     rel_src = src.relative_to(root)
>     rel_dest = candidate.relative_to(root)
>     print(f"  -> moving: {rel_src}  ==>  {rel_dest}")
>     shutil.move(str(src), str(candidate))
> 
> 
> def safe_copy(src: Path, dest: Path) -> None:
>     dest_parent = dest.parent
>     dest_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     candidate = dest
>     if candidate.exists():
>         stem = candidate.stem
>         suffix = candidate.suffix
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             if suffix:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}{suffix}"
>             else:
>                 new_name = f"{stem}__DUP{n}"
>             candidate = dest.with_name(new_name)
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     shutil.copy2(src, candidate)
> 
> 
> def write_client_meta(root: Path, client_name: str, client_code: str, qid: str, band: str | None = None) -> None:
>     meta = {
>         "client_name": client_name,
>         "client_code": client_code,
>         "qid": qid,
>         "band": band or "unassigned",
>         "created_at_utc": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
>         "root_path": str(root),
>     }
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if meta_path.exists():
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             candidate = root / f"client.meta__DUP{n}.json"
>             if not candidate.exists():
>                 meta_path = candidate
>                 break
>             n += 1
>     with meta_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>         json.dump(meta, f, indent=2)
>     print(f"[+] Wrote client meta: {meta_path.relative_to(root)}")
> 
> 
> def slug_from_name(name: str) -> str:
>     if not name.strip():
>         return "c.client"
>     words = [w for w in name.replace("_", " ").split() if w]
>     if not words:
>         return "c.client"
>     initials = "".join(w[0].lower() for w in words[:3])
>     return f"c.{initials}"
> 
> 
> def scaffold_kb_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     kb_root = root / "kb_site"
>     readme = kb_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Knowledge Base Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's portable KB site (e.g. Starlight, Docusaurus, etc.).
> 
> Recommended:
> - /kb_site/src or /kb_site/docs for content
> - Integrate with QiOS/QiNote pipelines for automated sync
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: kb_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def scaffold_marketing_site(root: Path) -> None:
>     mkt_root = root / "marketing_site"
>     readme = mkt_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = """# Client Marketing Site
> 
> This folder is reserved for the client's marketing website project.
> 
> Recommended:
> - Use your standard QiAlly marketing template (e.g. Vite/React/Astro)
> - Connect to domain + Cloudflare/hosting of choice
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: marketing_site/README.md")
> 
> 
> def normalize_filename(filename: str) -> str:
>     p = Path(filename)
>     stem = p.stem.lower()
>     ext = p.suffix
> 
>     stem = re.sub(r"[ \t]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"[\\/]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\-_]+", "-", stem)
>     stem = re.sub(r"-{2,}", "-", stem).strip("-")
> 
>     return stem + ext
> 
> 
> # ====================================
> # === TEMPLATE RESOURCE SUPPORT   ====
> # ====================================
> 
> def copy_template_resources(client_root: Path) -> None:
>     """
>     Copy resources from TEMPLATE_ROOT into the new client repo
>     according to TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS.
>     Never overwrites; uses safe_copy.
>     """
>     if not TEMPLATE_ROOT.exists():
>         print("[!] TEMPLATE_ROOT does not exist; skipping template copy.")
>         return
> 
>     print("[*] Copying template resources into client repo...")
>     for src_rel, dest_rel in TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS.items():
>         src_dir = TEMPLATE_ROOT / src_rel
>         if not src_dir.exists():
>             print(f"  - Template subfolder missing, skipping: templates/{src_rel}")
>             continue
> 
>         for path in src_dir.rglob("*"):
>             if path.is_dir():
>                 continue
>             if ".git" in path.parts:
>                 continue
> 
>             rel_from_src = path.relative_to(src_dir)
>             dest_path = client_root / dest_rel / rel_from_src
>             safe_copy(path, dest_path)
>             print(f"  + copied: templates/{src_rel}/{rel_from_src} -> {dest_rel}/{rel_from_src}")
>     print("[✓] Template resources copied.\n")
> 
> 
> # ===========================================
> # === INTERACTIVE REORGANIZATION (LEGACY) ====
> # ===========================================
> 
> def interactive_reorganize_move_rules(root: Path) -> None:
>     print("[*] Stage 1: Legacy MOVE_RULES (exact root names).")
>     print("    I will NOT delete or overwrite anything.\n")
> 
>     for src_name, dest_rel in MOVE_RULES.items():
>         src = root / src_name
>         if not src.exists():
>             continue
> 
>         print(f"Found: {src_name}/  ->  proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>         choice = input("  Move this now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>         if choice == "y":
>             safe_move(root, src, dest_rel)
>         else:
>             print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Stage 1 (MOVE_RULES) completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize_patterns(root: Path, use_normalization: bool) -> None:
>     print("[*] Stage 2: Pattern-based organization (file/folder name patterns).")
>     print("    Scanning for non-canonical items that match pattern rules.\n")
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     canonical_roots = {Path(f).parts[0] for f in folders if f}
> 
>     ignore_names = {
>         "client.meta.json",
>         REGISTRY_PATH.name,
>         Path(__file__).name,
>     }
> 
>     for path in sorted(root.rglob("*")):
>         if path.is_dir() and path == root:
>             continue
> 
>         rel = path.relative_to(root)
>         rel_parts = rel.parts
> 
>         if rel_parts and (rel_parts[0] in canonical_roots or rel_parts[0] == "_system"):
>             continue
> 
>         if path.name in ignore_names:
>             continue
> 
>         name_lower = path.name.lower()
> 
>         for rule in PATTERN_RULES:
>             if any(substr in name_lower for substr in rule["contains"]):
>                 dest_dir = rule["dest"]
>                 label = rule.get("label", dest_dir)
>                 print(f"Pattern match [{label}]: {rel}")
> 
>                 if path.is_file():
>                     new_name = normalize_filename(path.name) if use_normalization else path.name
>                     dest_rel = str(Path(dest_dir) / new_name)
>                 else:
>                     dest_rel = str(Path(dest_dir) / path.name)
> 
>                 print(f"  Proposed destination: {dest_rel}")
>                 choice = input("  Move this item now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>                 if choice == "y":
>                     safe_move(root, path, dest_rel)
>                 else:
>                     print("  Skipped.\n")
> 
>                 break
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Stage 2 (PATTERN_RULES) completed.\n")
> 
> 
> def interactive_reorganize(root: Path) -> None:
>     interactive_reorganize_move_rules(root)
> 
>     norm_choice = input("Enable filename normalization for pattern-based moves? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>     use_normalization = norm_choice == "y"
> 
>     interactive_reorganize_patterns(root, use_normalization)
> 
>     print("[✓] Reorganization pass completed.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === MODES: NEW / CLEANUP  ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def mode_new_client() -> None:
>     print("\n=== NEW CLIENT SETUP ===")
> 
>     default_base = str(Path.cwd())
>     base_input = prompt_input("Base directory to create client folder in", default_base)
>     base_path = Path(base_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not base_path.exists():
>         print(f"Base path does not exist, creating: {base_path}")
>         base_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     client_name = prompt_input("Client display name (e.g. 'Built By Rays Construction')", "")
>     if not client_name:
>         print("Client name is required. Aborting.")
>         return
> 
>     default_code = slug_from_name(client_name)
>     client_code = prompt_input("Client code/folder name (e.g. 'c.bbr')", default_code)
>     if not client_code:
>         client_code = default_code
> 
>     band = prompt_input("Client band (e.g. 'gold', 'silver', 'standard')", "standard")
> 
>     client_root = base_path / client_code
>     if client_root.exists():
>         print(f"WARNING: {client_root} already exists.")
>         n = 1
>         while True:
>             alt = base_path / f"{client_code}__NEW{n}"
>             if not alt.exists():
>                 client_root = alt
>                 print(f"Using new folder instead: {client_root}")
>                 break
>             n += 1
> 
>     client_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     registry = load_registry()
>     qid = generate_qid_unique(registry)
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Creating client repo at: {client_root}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Name : {client_name}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Code : {client_code}")
>     print(f"[+] Client Band : {band}")
>     print(f"[+] QID         : {qid}\n")
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(client_root, folders)
> 
>     write_client_meta(client_root, client_name, client_code, qid, band)
>     register_client_in_registry(registry, qid, client_name, client_code, client_root, band)
> 
>     use_templates = prompt_input("Copy template resources from qi-client-template into this client? [Y/n]", "y").lower()
>     if use_templates in ("y", "yes", ""):
>         copy_template_resources(client_root)
> 
>     # Minimal scaffolds (only if template resources didn't drop their own README)
>     scaffold_kb_site(client_root)
>     scaffold_marketing_site(client_root)
> 
>     readme = client_root / "README.md"
>     if not readme.exists():
>         content = f"""# {client_name} ({client_code})
> 
> - QID: {qid}
> - Band: {band or 'standard'}
> - Created: {datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}Z
> 
> This is the portable QiAlly-style client workspace.
> """
>         readme.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
>         print("  + scaffolded: README.md")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] New client repo created.\n")
> 
> 
> def maybe_backfill_registry_from_meta(root: Path) -> None:
>     meta_path = root / "client.meta.json"
>     if not meta_path.exists():
>         return
> 
>     try:
>         with meta_path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
>             meta = json.load(f)
>     except Exception:
>         return
> 
>     qid = meta.get("qid")
>     if not qid:
>         return
> 
>     registry = load_registry()
>     if qid in registry_qids(registry):
>         return
> 
>     print(f"[!] client.meta.json found with QID {qid}, not in registry.")
>     choice = input("    Add this client to QID registry now? [y/N] ").strip().lower()
>     if choice != "y":
>         print("    Skipped registry backfill.\n")
>         return
> 
>     client_name = meta.get("client_name", "Unknown Client")
>     client_code = meta.get("client_code", "c.unknown")
>     band = meta.get("band", "unassigned")
>     register_client_in_registry(registry, qid, client_name, client_code, root, band)
>     print("    Registry backfilled from client.meta.json.\n")
> 
> 
> def mode_cleanup() -> None:
>     print("\n=== CLEAN UP EXISTING CLIENT FOLDERS ===")
> 
>     default_root = str(Path.cwd())
>     root_input = prompt_input("Existing client root path", default_root)
>     root = Path(root_input).expanduser().resolve()
>     if not root.exists():
>         print(f"ERROR: Path does not exist: {root}")
>         return
> 
>     print(f"\n[+] Operating on: {root}\n")
> 
>     maybe_backfill_registry_from_meta(root)
> 
>     folders = CLIENT_MANIFEST.get("folders", [])
>     if not folders:
>         print("ERROR: Manifest has no folders defined.")
>         return
> 
>     ensure_folders(root, folders)
>     interactive_reorganize(root)
> 
>     print("[✓] Cleanup done.\n")
> 
> 
> # ==============================
> # === ENTRYPOINT / MENU     ====
> # ==============================
> 
> def main() -> None:
>     print("=== QiAlly Client Spawner ===")
>     print("Template repo:", SCRIPT_DIR)
>     print("Registry file:", REGISTRY_PATH.name)
>     print()
>     print("This tool can either:")
>     print("  1) Create a NEW client repo (portable structure + QID + registry + templates)")
>     print("  2) Clean up / reorganize an EXISTING client repo\n")
> 
>     while True:
>         choice = prompt_input("Choose mode: [1] New client, [2] Cleanup, [Q] Quit", "1").lower()
>         if choice in ("1", "new", "n"):
>             mode_new_client()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("2", "cleanup", "c"):
>             mode_cleanup()
>             break
>         elif choice in ("q", "quit", "exit"):
>             print("Bye.")
>             return
>         else:
>             print("Invalid choice, try again.\n")
> 
> 
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>     main()
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> If you want a tiny `start.sh` wrapper next so you can just run it without thinking (`./start.sh` → menu pops), I can draft that too.

### User
> yes,

### Assistant
> Cool. Here’s your little launcher.
> 
> Put this `start.sh` in the **root** of `qi-client-template` (same place as `client_spawner.py`).
> 
> ```bash
> #!/usr/bin/env bash
> # QiAlly Client Spawner launcher
> # Lives in the qi-client-template repo root
> 
> set -e
> 
> # Resolve repo root (directory of this script)
> SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
> 
> SPAWNER="$SCRIPT_DIR/client_spawner.py"
> 
> if [ ! -f "$SPAWNER" ]; then
>   echo "ERROR: client_spawner.py not found at: $SPAWNER"
>   exit 1
> fi
> 
> # Try python3 first, then python
> if command -v python3 >/dev/null 2>&1; then
>   PYTHON_BIN="python3"
> elif command -v python >/dev/null 2>&1; then
>   PYTHON_BIN="python"
> else
>   echo "ERROR: Python is not installed or not on PATH."
>   exit 1
> fi
> 
> echo "----------------------------------------"
> echo " QiAlly Client Spawner (Template Repo)  "
> echo "----------------------------------------"
> echo "Repo root : $SCRIPT_DIR"
> echo "Spawner   : $SPAWNER"
> echo "Python    : $PYTHON_BIN"
> echo
> 
> # Run the spawner
> "$PYTHON_BIN" "$SPAWNER"
> ```
> 
> Then:
> 
> ```bash
> cd /path/to/qi-client-template
> chmod +x start.sh
> ./start.sh
> ```
> 
> Flow you’ll see:
> 
> 1. Wrapper resolves repo root  
> 2. Runs `client_spawner.py`  
> 3. Spawner asks: **New client** or **Cleanup existing**  
> 4. You point it at the external path, it does its thing and only touches:
>    - the client folder  
>    - `qi_client_registry.json` in the template repo  
> 
> If you also want a Windows `.bat` launcher for when you’re on the laptop without WSL, say the word.

> word, and what other improves or automations can we make so the template needs to already have a ready to build kp site and client portal deployed automitcally the first time ect. this agent should be create an agent for the client too to handle maintenance and updates and control the file to like self heal.

### Assistant
> Yeah, now you’re talking “mini-OS per client,” not just folders.
> 
> Let’s zoom this out into **what should exist** and **what to automate next**.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 1. Make the template repo truly “ready-to-launch”
> 
> Right now it’s just structure + docs. You want:
> 
> ### a) kb_site: ready-to-build static KB
> 
> In `templates/kb_site/`:
> 
> - Pick a stack and stick to it:
>   - e.g. **Starlight** or **Docusaurus**, or even just Vite + Markdown.
> - Have:
>   - `package.json`
>   - `src/` or `docs/`
>   - `starlight.config.mts` / `docusaurus.config.js` with **placeholders**:
>     - `CLIENT_NAME`
>     - `CLIENT_CODE`
>     - `QID`
>     - `PRIMARY_DOMAIN`
> - Add a simple `kb.env.template`:
>   ```env
>   KB_SITE_TITLE=CLIENT_NAME Knowledge Base
>   KB_SITE_URL=https://kb.CLIENT_CODE.qially.app
>   KB_SITE_QID=QID_PLACEHOLDER
>   ```
> - The spawner can:
>   - Copy kb_site
>   - Do a quick string replace on `CLIENT_NAME`, `CLIENT_CODE`, `QID` in config + env.
> 
> That gives you **per-client KB ready to `npm install && npm run build && deploy`** with no manual rename.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### b) client portal: ready-to-deploy QiPortal shell
> 
> In `templates/marketing_site/` or `templates/client_portal/`:
> 
> - Base it on your existing **QiPortals** stack (Vite/React + CF).
> - Include:
>   - `wrangler.toml.template`
>   - `portal.env.template`
>   - `src/config/clientConfig.ts` with placeholders:
>     ```ts
>     export const CLIENT_QID = "QID_PLACEHOLDER";
>     export const CLIENT_CODE = "CLIENT_CODE_PLACEHOLDER";
>     export const CLIENT_NAME = "CLIENT_NAME_PLACEHOLDER";
>     ```
> - Spawner:
>   - Copies portal folder
>   - Replaces placeholders (same as kb_site)
> 
> Now **every new client** comes with:
> 
> - KB skeleton
> - Portal skeleton
> - Both already tagged with that client’s **QID**.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 2. Upgrade the spawner into a “one-click scaffolder”
> 
> Right now it:
> 
> - asks: new vs cleanup  
> - asks for path  
> - creates structure  
> - copies templates  
> - writes meta + registry  
> 
> Next upgrades:
> 
> ### a) Smarter intake questions (NEW mode)
> 
> After name/code/band, add:
> 
> - `Primary domain? (optional, e.g. raysconstruction.com)`
> - `KB subdomain? (e.g. kb.raysconstruction.com)`
> - `Portal subdomain? (e.g. portal.raysconstruction.com)`
> - `Client contact email?`
> - `Internal owner? (Which Qi user is responsible?)`
> 
> Store all that in `client.meta.json`, e.g.:
> 
> ```json
> {
>   "client_name": "Built By Rays Construction",
>   "client_code": "c.bbr",
>   "qid": "QCL-20251206-ABCD",
>   "band": "gold",
>   "kb_domain": "kb.raysconstruction.com",
>   "portal_domain": "portal.raysconstruction.com",
>   "primary_domain": "raysconstruction.com",
>   "contact_email": "luis@raysconstruction.com",
>   "owner": "Cody",
>   "created_at_utc": "..."
> }
> ```
> 
> This becomes your **single source of truth** for other automations.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### b) “Do you want me to prep deployments?” step
> 
> Still no API keys in the spawner (smart), but it can **generate scripts** inside the client repo:
> 
> - `/kb_site/prepare.sh`
> - `/marketing_site/prepare.sh` or `/portal/prepare.sh`
> 
> Example for KB:
> 
> ```bash
> #!/usr/bin/env bash
> set -e
> cd "$(dirname "$0")"
> npm install
> npm run build
> echo "Now run your deploy command (Cloudflare Pages / Netlify / etc)."
> ```
> 
> Example for portal (Cloudflare):
> 
> ```bash
> #!/usr/bin/env bash
> set -e
> cd "$(dirname "$0")"
> cp wrangler.toml.template wrangler.toml
> # maybe sed replace domain placeholder if you want
> npm install
> npm run build
> npx wrangler deploy
> ```
> 
> Spawner doesn’t deploy. It merely **drops the scripts and fills in config**.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 3. Introduce a per-client “agent” script
> 
> You’re asking for:
> 
> > “agent for the client too to handle maintenance and updates and control the file to like self heal.”
> 
> Cool. That’s basically a **`client_agent.py`** that lives *inside each client repo*.
> 
> Spawner can:
> 
> - Copy `templates/client_agent/client_agent.py` → `<client_root>/client_agent.py`
> - Customize with the client’s QID + root.
> 
> Example capabilities for `client_agent.py`:
> 
> ```bash
> python client_agent.py healthcheck
> python client_agent.py reconcile
> python client_agent.py sync-kb
> python client_agent.py report
> ```
> 
> ### Agent behaviors
> 
> 1. **Healthcheck**
>    - Compare actual folder structure vs `CLIENT_MANIFEST`.
>    - Report:
>      - Missing folders
>      - Empty critical folders
>      - Orphan files sitting at root (e.g. random PDFs).
>    - Output `reports/healthcheck_YYYYMMDD.md`.
> 
> 2. **Reconcile / Self-heal**
>    - Re-run the **same manifest logic** (ensure folders).
>    - Optionally:
>      - Move obvious misfiled items using PATTERN_RULES automatically (no prompt).
>      - Add a `--dry-run` flag.
> 
> 3. **KB sync**
>    - (Later) integrate with QiNote / QiVault:
>      - Import new markdown notes into `kb_site/` or `60_resources/kb_vault`.
>      - Regenerate a simple index page.
> 
> 4. **Report**
>    - Summarize:
>      - Total files, size by major folder.
>      - Last modified times for important areas.
>    - Useful for “is this client cold or active?” quick read.
> 
> Spawner’s job is just to **drop** that agent into the client and wire its config from `client.meta.json`. You then run the agent when you feel like healing things.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 4. Make the registry more powerful (without extra complexity)
> 
> You already keep `qi_client_registry.json` in the template repo.
> 
> Upgrades:
> 
> 1. Add fields for:
>    - `status` (`active`, `paused`, `archived`, `lead`)
>    - `services` (list, e.g. `["kb", "portal", "bookkeeping"]`)
>    - `notes` (short string).
> 2. Add a **new CLI mode in the spawner**: `Registry view`
> 
> When you run `start.sh`:
> 
> - Option 3: `View registry / search`
>   - List last N clients
>   - Filter by band or status
>   - Search by name, QID, or code
> 
> That keeps it as a lightweight **CLI mini-CRM** with no extra tools.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 5. Guardrails so this doesn’t turn into a monster
> 
> You’re already on the edge of “too much magic.” To keep it sane:
> 
> - **Spawner does only:**
>   - Intake questions
>   - Structure creation
>   - Template copy
>   - Meta + registry updates
> - **Agent does:**
>   - Ongoing care + self-healing **inside** a client repo
> - **Template repo does:**
>   - Source of truth for:
>     - KB skeleton
>     - Portal skeleton
>     - Agent skeleton
>     - Docs, SOPs, email templates, etc.
> 
> You update templates manually, commit changes, and every new client gets the improved baseline. Old clients can be “patched” by running the **agent** or a future “upgrade templates” command.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Concrete next steps
> 
> If you want to move fast without chaos, next moves:
> 
> 1. **In `qi-client-template/templates/`:**
>    - Add:
>      - `kb_site/` with a real Starlight or Docusaurus starter.
>      - `client_portal/` or reuse `marketing_site/` with your QiPortal shell.
>      - `client_agent/client_agent.py` skeleton.
> 2. I’ll:
>    - Update `client_spawner.py` to:
>      - Ask for domains + email.
>      - Do placeholder replacement in kb & portal configs.
>      - Copy `client_agent.py` into each new client.
>    - Sketch a basic `client_agent.py` with `healthcheck` + `reconcile` commands wired to your manifest.
> 
> You’ll end up with:
> 
> - `git clone qi-client-template`
> - `./start.sh`
> - Answer a few questions → **full client OS** scaffolded:
>   - KB, portal, structure, meta, registry, and a little maintenance bot ready to run.
> 
> If you want, I can jump straight into the **`client_agent.py` skeleton + the placeholder-replacement code** in the spawner next.

### User
> lets keep it flat, light, and portable, lets strive for html5, avoid heavy or deep anything, and validations that run to keep file folder bloating down and auto compressionand such.

### Assistant
> Yup, good call. You’re flirting with “mini-Kubernetes per client,” and you do *not* need that. Let’s strip this down.
> 
> ### Design rules going forward
> 
> 1. **Flat & portable**
>    - Folders: shallow, predictable, no deep trees.
>    - Everything should move with a simple `zip` or drag-and-drop.
>    - No dependency on a specific host, runtime, or DB just to *view* core content.
> 
> 2. **HTML5 first**
>    - Client KB and portal: simple HTML5 + a bit of vanilla JS if needed.
>    - No React, no Vite, no Node build required to *use* it.
>    - Optional “enhanced” variants can exist later, but base should be just:
>      - `index.html`
>      - `/assets`
>      - `/css`
>      - `/js` (optional)
> 
> 3. **Agents do hygiene, not heroics**
>    - One `client_agent.py` per client repo.
>    - Jobs:
>      - Validate structure and bloat.
>      - Compress / archive heavy stuff.
>      - Normalize filenames.
>    - No magical deployments, no external APIs baked in.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 1. Template repo: keep it light
> 
> Update `qi-client-template` like this:
> 
> ```text
> qi-client-template/
> ├── client_spawner.py
> ├── start.sh
> ├── qi_client_registry.json              # auto-managed by spawner
> └── templates/
>     ├── kb_site/                         # flat HTML5 KB shell
>     │   ├── index.html
>     │   ├── css/
>     │   │   └── style.css
>     │   └── assets/
>     ├── portal_shell/                    # simple HTML5 client portal shell
>     │   ├── index.html
>     │   ├── css/
>     │   └── js/
>     ├── system_templates/                # emails, SOPs, docs, etc.
>     ├── kb_vault_seed/                   # starter markdown / docs
>     └── client_agent/
>         └── client_agent.py              # copied into each client repo
> ```
> 
> Then adjust `TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS` in `client_spawner.py`:
> 
> ```python
> TEMPLATE_MAPPINGS = {
>     "kb_site": "kb_site",
>     "portal_shell": "portal",
>     "system_templates": "_system/templates",
>     "kb_vault_seed": "60_resources/kb_vault",
>     "client_agent": ".",  # drops client_agent.py into client root
> }
> ```
> 
> No build chain. Just raw HTML/CSS/JS and markdown.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 2. HTML5 KB + portal behavior
> 
> **KB (`kb_site/`)**
> 
> - `index.html`:
>   - Reads a simple JSON or embeds links to docs under `60_resources/kb_vault`.
>   - You can keep it dumb at first: static “Welcome & Links” page.
> - Optionally later:
>   - A tiny JS script that:
>     - Lists `.md` or `.html` docs from a known folder (if you want a richer view, but we can skip for now).
> 
> **Portal (`portal/`)**
> 
> - `index.html`:
>   - Simple nav:
>     - **KB** → `../kb_site/index.html`
>     - **Docs** → `../60_resources`
>     - **External links** → Zoho portal, booking, etc.
>   - Shows basic client info (from `client.meta.json` if you want to embed later via a tiny JS script).
> 
> The point: Everything opens in any browser, no backend required.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 3. Validation + bloat control (the “self-heal” part)
> 
> This belongs in **`client_agent.py`** inside the client repo.
> 
> Keep it small and CLI-style:
> 
> ```bash
> python client_agent.py validate
> python client_agent.py compact
> python client_agent.py report
> ```
> 
> ### a) Validation (`validate`)
> 
> Checks:
> 
> - All manifest folders exist.
> - Warns on:
>   - Files at root that don’t belong (`*.tmp`, random downloads).
>   - Depth > 4 (`root/a/b/c/d/e` → red flag).
> - Optional: Ensure certain key files exist:
>   - `client.meta.json`
>   - `README.md`
>   - `kb_site/index.html`
>   - `portal/index.html`
> 
> ### b) Compact (`compact`)
> 
> Strategies:
> 
> - **Large file detection**
>   - Find any file > e.g. 25 MB.
>   - Move them into `70_archive/large_assets/` and leave a `.pointer` text file where it used to be.
> - **Archive old folders**
>   - If you mark a folder as “cold” (e.g. `50_casework/old_*`), compress to `.zip` in `70_archive/`.
> - **Images**
>   - If PIL / pillow is available, you *can* optionally:
>     - Re-encode giant JPEGs down to a reasonable size.
>   - If not, just flag them and move to `large_assets`.
> 
> ### c) Report (`report`)
> 
> - Summarize:
>   - Total size by top-level folder.
>   - Top 10 largest files.
>   - Count of files by type (`.pdf`, `.jpg`, `.md`, etc).
> - Output to:
>   - `70_archive/reports/health_YYYYMMDD_HHMM.html` (simple HTML5 report).
>   - Keep it static and viewable anywhere.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 4. Example: lightweight `client_agent.py` skeleton
> 
> This stays **inside** the client repo and does not touch the template repo.
> 
> You can drop this in `templates/client_agent/client_agent.py` and let the spawner copy it over:
> 
> ```python
> #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> QiAlly Client Agent (lightweight)
> 
> Commands:
>   - validate   : check structure + bloat signals
>   - compact    : move/zip heavy stuff to archive
>   - report     : generate simple HTML report
> 
> Usage:
>   python client_agent.py validate
>   python client_agent.py compact
>   python client_agent.py report
> """
> 
> import sys
> import json
> import shutil
> import zipfile
> from pathlib import Path
> from datetime import datetime
> 
> ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
> META_PATH = ROOT / "client.meta.json"
> 
> # Shallow manifest: only care about TOP-LEVEL folders here.
> REQUIRED_TOP_LEVEL = [
>     "_system",
>     "10_profile",
>     "20_engagement",
>     "30_operations",
>     "40_finance",
>     "50_casework",
>     "60_resources",
>     "70_archive",
>     "kb_site",
>     "portal",
> ]
> 
> LARGE_FILE_MB = 25
> 
> 
> def load_meta() -> dict:
>     if META_PATH.exists():
>         try:
>             return json.loads(META_PATH.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
>         except Exception:
>             pass
>     return {}
> 
> 
> def validate() -> int:
>     print("=== VALIDATE ===")
>     meta = load_meta()
>     if meta:
>         print(f"Client: {meta.get('client_name', 'Unknown')} ({meta.get('client_code', 'c.unknown')})")
>         print(f"QID   : {meta.get('qid', 'N/A')}")
>     else:
>         print("WARN: client.meta.json missing or unreadable.")
> 
>     print("\n[1] Top-level folders")
>     missing = []
>     for name in REQUIRED_TOP_LEVEL:
>         p = ROOT / name
>         if not p.exists():
>             missing.append(name)
>             print(f"  - MISSING : {name}")
>         else:
>             print(f"  - OK      : {name}")
> 
>     print("\n[2] Orphan files at root (non-ignored)")
>     ignored = {"client.meta.json", "README.md", "client_agent.py"}
>     orphans = []
>     for item in ROOT.iterdir():
>         if item.is_file() and item.name not in ignored:
>             orphans.append(item.name)
>             print(f"  - ORPHAN FILE: {item.name}")
> 
>     print("\n[3] Depth check (anything deeper than 4 levels)")
>     too_deep = []
>     max_depth = 4
>     for path in ROOT.rglob("*"):
>         rel = path.relative_to(ROOT)
>         depth = len(rel.parts)
>         if depth > max_depth:
>             too_deep.append(str(rel))
> 
>     if too_deep:
>         print(f"Found {len(too_deep)} items deeper than {max_depth} levels:")
>         for rel in too_deep[:20]:
>             print(f"  - {rel}")
>         if len(too_deep) > 20:
>             print(f"  ... +{len(too_deep) - 20} more")
>     else:
>         print("No paths beyond depth limit.")
> 
>     print("\n[4] Large files (>{} MB)".format(LARGE_FILE_MB))
>     large = []
>     threshold = LARGE_FILE_MB * 1024 * 1024
>     for path in ROOT.rglob("*"):
>         if path.is_file():
>             try:
>                 size = path.stat().st_size
>             except OSError:
>                 continue
>             if size >= threshold:
>                 large.append((path, size))
> 
>     if large:
>         for path, size in sorted(large, key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True):
>             rel = path.relative_to(ROOT)
>             mb = size / (1024 * 1024)
>             print(f"  - {rel} ({mb:.1f} MB)")
>     else:
>         print("No large files found.")
> 
>     print("\n[✓] Validation complete.\n")
>     return 0
> 
> 
> def compact() -> int:
>     print("=== COMPACT ===")
>     archive_root = ROOT / "70_archive"
>     archive_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     # 1) Move large files into 70_archive/large_assets and leave pointer
>     large_assets_dir = archive_root / "large_assets"
>     large_assets_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
> 
>     threshold = LARGE_FILE_MB * 1024 * 1024
>     moved = 0
> 
>     for path in ROOT.rglob("*"):
>         if not path.is_file():
>             continue
>         if path.is_relative_to(archive_root):
>             continue
>         if path.name in {"client.meta.json", "client_agent.py"}:
>             continue
> 
>         try:
>             size = path.stat().st_size
>         except OSError:
>             continue
> 
>         if size >= threshold:
>             rel = path.relative_to(ROOT)
>             target = large_assets_dir / rel
>             target.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>             print(f"  - Moving large file to archive: {rel}")
>             shutil.move(str(path), str(target))
>             moved += 1
> 
>             pointer_path = ROOT / rel
>             pointer_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>             pointer_path.write_text(
>                 f"This file was moved to archive:\n"
>                 f"  70_archive/large_assets/{rel}\n"
>                 f"Size: {size / (1024*1024):.1f} MB\n",
>                 encoding="utf-8",
>             )
> 
>     print(f"\n[✓] Compact complete. Large files moved: {moved}\n")
>     return 0
> 
> 
> def report() -> int:
>     print("=== REPORT ===")
>     meta = load_meta()
>     now = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC")
>     summary = {
>         "generated_at": now,
>         "client": {
>             "name": meta.get("client_name", "Unknown"),
>             "code": meta.get("client_code", "c.unknown"),
>             "qid": meta.get("qid", "N/A"),
>         },
>         "folders": {},
>         "largest_files": [],
>     }
> 
>     # Folder size summary
>     for top in ROOT.iterdir():
>         if not top.is_dir():
>             continue
>         size = 0
>         count = 0
>         for path in top.rglob("*"):
>             if path.is_file():
>                 try:
>                     size += path.stat().st_size
>                     count += 1
>                 except OSError:
>                     continue
>         summary["folders"][top.name] = {
>             "files": count,
>             "size_bytes": size,
>         }
> 
>     # Largest files
>     all_files = []
>     for path in ROOT.rglob("*"):
>         if path.is_file():
>             try:
>                 size = path.stat().st_size
>             except OSError:
>                 continue
>             all_files.append((path, size))
> 
>     top_n = sorted(all_files, key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:20]
>     for path, size in top_n:
>         rel = path.relative_to(ROOT)
>         summary["largest_files"].append(
>             {"path": str(rel), "size_bytes": size}
>         )
> 
>     # Write HTML report
>     reports_dir = ROOT / "70_archive" / "reports"
>     reports_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
>     ts = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
>     html_path = reports_dir / f"health_{ts}.html"
> 
>     def fmt_size(b: int) -> str:
>         mb = b / (1024 * 1024)
>         return f"{mb:.1f} MB"
> 
>     lines = []
>     lines.append("<!DOCTYPE html>")
>     lines.append("<html><head><meta charset='utf-8'><title>Client Health Report</title>")
>     lines.append("<style>body{font-family:sans-serif;max-width:900px;margin:2rem auto;} table{border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;} th,td{border:1px solid #ccc;padding:4px 8px;text-align:left;} h1,h2{margin-top:1.5rem;}</style>")
>     lines.append("</head><body>")
>     lines.append(f"<h1>Client Health Report</h1>")
>     lines.append(f"<p>Generated: {now}</p>")
>     lines.append(f"<p>Client: {summary['client']['name']} ({summary['client']['code']}) – QID: {summary['client']['qid']}</p>")
> 
>     lines.append("<h2>Folder Summary</h2>")
>     lines.append("<table><tr><th>Folder</th><th>Files</th><th>Size</th></tr>")
>     for name, info in sorted(summary["folders"].items()):
>         lines.append(f"<tr><td>{name}</td><td>{info['files']}</td><td>{fmt_size(info['size_bytes'])}</td></tr>")
>     lines.append("</table>")
> 
>     lines.append("<h2>Largest Files</h2>")
>     if summary["largest_files"]:
>         lines.append("<table><tr><th>Path</th><th>Size</th></tr>")
>         for item in summary["largest_files"]:
>             lines.append(f"<tr><td>{item['path']}</td><td>{fmt_size(item['size_bytes'])}</td></tr>")
>         lines.append("</table>")
>     else:
>         lines.append("<p>No files found.</p>")
> 
>     lines.append("</body></html>")
>     html_path.write_text("\n".join(lines), encoding="utf-8")
> 
>     print(f"[✓] Report written to: {html_path}")
>     return 0
> 
> 
> def main(argv: list[str]) -> int:
>     if len(argv) < 2:
>         print("Usage: python client_agent.py [validate|compact|report]")
>         return 1
> 
>     cmd = argv[1].lower()
>     if cmd == "validate":
>         return validate()
>     if cmd == "compact":
>         return compact()
>     if cmd == "report":
>         return report()
> 
>     print(f"Unknown command: {cmd}")
>     return 1
> 
> 
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>     raise SystemExit(main(sys.argv))
> ```
> 
> That’s it. Lightweight, no external deps, pure Python + HTML.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 5. Where this leaves us
> 
> - **Spawner**: lives in template repo, stays simple:
>   - Creates structure
>   - Copies flat HTML5 shells + client_agent
>   - Writes meta + registry
> - **Client repo**: is portable:
>   - HTML KB
>   - HTML portal shell
>   - Python agent that keeps it clean, small, and shallow
> - **No heavy frameworks** unless *you* consciously opt-in for a specific client project.
> 
> If you want, next we can tighten the **manifest** itself to be a bit flatter (some of those nested 50_casework paths can be collapsed one level) so the system actually lives by your “no deep anything” rule.

### User
> lets tighten the manifest work on the client agent, and of course the portal RAG agent very light self contained.

### Assistant
> Good, this is the right constraint: **flat, light, portable**.
> 
> I’ll give you three pieces:
> 
> 1. Tightened **manifest** (shallow, generic, still powerful).  
> 2. Updated **client_agent.py** wired to that manifest (validate / compact / report / build_index).  
> 3. A tiny **portal RAG agent**: pure HTML+JS search over a static JSON index the agent builds.
> 
> You can plug these straight into your template repo.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 1. Tight, shallow client manifest
> 
> Goal:  
> - No deep nesting.  
> - Generic across use cases (immigration, tax, ops, marketing).  
> - Plays well with HTML5 + local files.
> 
> ### Proposed top-level layout
> 
> ```text
> <client_root>/
> ├── _system/          # tools, scripts, logs, internal-only
> ├── 10_profile/       # who this client is
> ├── 20_engagement/    # how you're engaged with them
> ├── 30_ops/           # day-to-day operations / sops / access
> ├── 40_finance/       # money, period
> ├── 50_work/          # actual work product / matters / projects
> ├── 60_kb/            # knowledge base + references
> ├── 70_archive/       # cold storage, zips, large assets, reports
> ├── kb_site/          # static HTML5 KB shell
> └── portal/           # static HTML5 “portal” shell
> ```
> 
> ### With one more level of structure (max depth 3)
> 
> ```python
> CLIENT_MANIFEST = {
>     "version": 2,
>     "description": "Flat QiAlly client structure (portable, shallow).",
>     "folders": [
>         # Internal/system
>         "_system",
>         "_system/logs",
>         "_system/scripts",
>         "_system/tools",
>         "_system/workers",
>         "_system/templates",
>         "_system/legacy",
> 
>         # 10_profile – who this client is
>         "10_profile",
>         "10_profile/ids",
>         "10_profile/personal",
> 
>         # 20_engagement – how you're engaged
>         "20_engagement",
>         "20_engagement/proposals",
>         "20_engagement/contracts",
>         "20_engagement/scope",
>         "20_engagement/policies",
>         "20_engagement/expectations",
>         "20_engagement/notes",
> 
>         # 30_ops – day-to-day ops + access
>         "30_ops",
>         "30_ops/onboarding",
>         "30_ops/access",
>         "30_ops/checklists",
>         "30_ops/sops",
>         "30_ops/notes",
> 
>         # 40_finance – money
>         "40_finance",
>         "40_finance/invoices",
>         "40_finance/expenses",
>         "40_finance/bank",
>         "40_finance/assets",
>         "40_finance/tax",
>         "40_finance/reports",
> 
>         # 50_work – actual work (streams/matters live here)
>         "50_work",                # e.g. 50_work/immigration, 50_work/marketing, etc.
> 
>         # 60_kb – knowledge base + references
>         "60_kb",
>         "60_kb/kb_vault",         # markdown/html notes
>         "60_kb/references",
>         "60_kb/media",
>         "60_kb/legal",
>         "60_kb/marketing",
>         "60_kb/training",
> 
>         # 70_archive – cold / heavy / snapshots
>         "70_archive",
>         "70_archive/large_assets",
>         "70_archive/reports",
>         "70_archive/snapshots",
> 
>         # HTML5 shells
>         "kb_site",
>         "portal",
>     ],
> }
> ```
> 
> You can drop that directly into `client_spawner.py` in place of the old manifest.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 2. Updated `client_agent.py` (aligned to the flat manifest + RAG index)
> 
> This goes in your template repo under:
> 
> `templates/client_agent/client_agent.py`
>
